# │   └── metrics.py
# └── main.py

# main.py - Ponto de entrada principal
import time
import json
import logging
from typing import Dict, Any, Optional, List
from contextlib import asynccontextmanager
from datetime import datetime, timedelta

import redis.asyncio as redis
from fastapi import FastAPI, Depends, HTTPException, status, Request, Response
from fastapi.middleware.cors import CORSMiddleware
from fastapi.responses import JSONResponse
from sqlalchemy.ext.asyncio import AsyncSession, create_async_engine
from sqlalchemy.orm import sessionmaker
import strawberry
from strawberry.fastapi import GraphQLRouter

# Configuração
from core.config import settings
from core.cache import RedisCache, CacheManager
from core.database import get_db, Base
from api.middleware.auth import AuthMiddleware, get_current_user
from api.middleware.cache import CacheMiddleware
from api.middleware.rate_limit import RateLimitMiddleware
from api.middleware.logging import StructuredLoggingMiddleware
from api.rest.v1.routers import api_router as rest_v1_router
from api.rest.v2.routers import api_router as rest_v2_router
from api.graphql.schema import schema as graphql_schema
from utils.logger import setup_logger
from utils.metrics import MetricsCollector

# Configurar logger
logger = setup_logger(__name__)

# Inicializar métricas
metrics = MetricsCollector()

# Lifespan manager para inicialização e cleanup
@asynccontextmanager
async def lifespan(app: FastAPI):
    """Gerencia ciclo de vida da aplicação"""
    startup_time = time.time()
    
    # Inicializar Redis
    app.state.redis_client = redis.from_url(
        settings.REDIS_URL,
        encoding="utf-8",
        decode_responses=True
    )
    app.state.cache_manager = CacheManager(app.state.redis_client)
    
    # Inicializar banco de dados
    engine = create_async_engine(settings.DATABASE_URL, echo=settings.DEBUG)
    async with engine.begin() as conn:
        await conn.run_sync(Base.metadata.create_all)
    
    app.state.db_engine = engine
    app.state.async_session = sessionmaker(
        engine, class_=AsyncSession, expire_on_commit=False
    )
    
    # Health check inicial
    await app.state.cache_manager.set("app_startup", str(startup_time), expire=300)
    
    logger.info("Application startup complete", extra={
        "startup_time_ms": int((time.time() - startup_time) * 1000)
    })
    
    yield
    
    # Cleanup
    await app.state.redis_client.close()
    await app.state.db_engine.dispose()
    
    logger.info("Application shutdown complete")

# Criar aplicação FastAPI
app = FastAPI(
    title="DIYAPP Evolution V11 API",
    description="APIs de Nova Geração - GraphQL/REST híbrido com cache Redis",
    version="2.0.0",
    lifespan=lifespan,
    docs_url="/api/docs",
    redoc_url="/api/redoc",
    openapi_url="/api/openapi.json"
)

# Configurar CORS
app.add_middleware(
    CORSMiddleware,
    allow_origins=settings.ALLOWED_ORIGINS,
    allow_credentials=True,
    allow_methods=["*"],
    allow_headers=["*"],
)

# Middlewares customizados
app.add_middleware(StructuredLoggingMiddleware)
app.add_middleware(AuthMiddleware)
app.add_middleware(CacheMiddleware)
app.add_middleware(RateLimitMiddleware)

# Configurar GraphQL
graphql_app = GraphQLRouter(graphql_schema, context_getter=lambda: {"db": app.state.async_session()})

# Rotas
app.include_router(rest_v1_router, prefix="/api/v1", tags=["REST v1"])
app.include_router(rest_v2_router, prefix="/api/v2", tags=["REST v2"])
app.include_router(graphql_app, prefix="/graphql", tags=["GraphQL"])

# Health Checks Detalhados
@app.get("/health", tags=["Health"])
async def health_check():
    """Health check básico"""
    return {"status": "healthy", "timestamp": datetime.utcnow().isoformat()}

@app.get("/health/detailed", tags=["Health"])
async def detailed_health_check(
    request: Request,
    db: AsyncSession = Depends(get_db)
):
    """Health check detalhado com verificação de dependências"""
    health_status = {
        "status": "healthy",
        "timestamp": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
        "checks": {}
    }
    
    # Verificar Redis
    try:
        start = time.time()
        await request.app.state.redis_client.ping()
        redis_latency = (time.time() - start) * 1000
        health_status["checks"]["redis"] = {
            "status": "healthy",
            "latency_ms": round(redis_latency, 2)
        }
    except Exception as e:
        health_status["checks"]["redis"] = {
            "status": "unhealthy",
            "error": str(e)
        }
        health_status["status"] = "degraded"
    
    # Verificar Database
    try:
        start = time.time()
        await db.execute("SELECT 1")
        db_latency = (time.time() - start) * 1000
        health_status["checks"]["database"] = {
            "status": "healthy",
            "latency_ms": round(db_latency, 2)
        }
    except Exception as e:
        health_status["checks"]["database"] = {
            "status": "unhealthy",
            "error": str(e)
        }
        health_status["status"] = "degraded"
    
    # Métricas do sistema
    health_status["metrics"] = {
        "active_connections": metrics.get_active_connections(),
        "request_rate": metrics.get_request_rate(),
        "error_rate": metrics.get_error_rate(),
        "cache_hit_rate": await request.app.state.cache_manager.get_hit_rate()
    }
    
    return health_status

@app.get("/metrics", tags=["Metrics"])
async def get_metrics():
    """Endpoint para coletar métricas (compatível com Prometheus)"""
    metrics_data = metrics.collect_all()
    return Response(
        content=metrics_data,
        media_type="text/plain"
    )

# Error handlers
@app.exception_handler(HTTPException)
async def http_exception_handler(request: Request, exc: HTTPException):
    """Handler global para HTTP exceptions"""
    logger.warning("HTTP Exception", extra={
        "path": request.url.path,
        "method": request.method,
        "status_code": exc.status_code,
        "detail": exc.detail
    })
    
    return JSONResponse(
        status_code=exc.status_code,
        content={
            "error": {
                "code": exc.status_code,
                "message": exc.detail,
                "timestamp": datetime.utcnow().isoformat()
            }
        }
    )

@app.exception_handler(Exception)
async def global_exception_handler(request: Request, exc: Exception):
    """Handler global para exceptions não tratadas"""
    error_id = f"err_{int(time.time())}"
    logger.error("Unhandled Exception", extra={
        "error_id": error_id,
        "path": request.url.path,
        "method": request.method,
        "error_type": type(exc).__name__,
        "error_message": str(exc),
        "traceback": logging.Formatter().formatException(exc.__traceback__)
    })
    
    # Incrementar métrica de erro
    metrics.increment_error()
    
    return JSONResponse(
        status_code=status.HTTP_500_INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR,
        content={
            "error": {
                "code": "INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR",
                "message": "An unexpected error occurred",
                "reference_id": error_id,
                "timestamp": datetime.utcnow().isoformat()
            }
        }
    )

# core/cache.py - Sistema de cache com Redis
import asyncio
from typing import Any, Optional, Union, Callable
from functools import wraps
import pickle
import hashlib

class RedisCache:
    """Wrapper para Redis com circuit breaker e fallback"""
    
    def __init__(self, redis_client, circuit_breaker_threshold: int = 5):
        self.redis = redis_client
        self.circuit_breaker_threshold = circuit_breaker_threshold
        self.failure_count = 0
        self.circuit_open = False
        self.circuit_open_until = None
        self.circuit_reset_timeout = 60  # segundos
        
    async def get(self, key: str) -> Optional[Any]:
        """Get com circuit breaker"""
        if self.circuit_open:
            if self.circuit_open_until and datetime.utcnow() < self.circuit_open_until:
                raise Exception("Circuit breaker open")
            else:
                self.circuit_open = False
                self.failure_count = 0
        
        try:
            result = await self.redis.get(key)
            if result:
                return pickle.loads(result.encode('latin1'))
            return None
        except Exception as e:
            self.failure_count += 1
            if self.failure_count >= self.circuit_breaker_threshold:
                self.circuit_open = True
                self.circuit_open_until = datetime.utcnow() + timedelta(seconds=self.circuit_reset_timeout)
            raise e
    
    async def set(self, key: str, value: Any, expire: int = 300) -> bool:
        """Set com circuit breaker"""
        if self.circuit_open:
            return False
        
        try:
            serialized = pickle.dumps(value).decode('latin1')
            await self.redis.setex(key, expire, serialized)
            self.failure_count = 0
            return True
        except Exception as e:
            self.failure_count += 1
            if self.failure_count >= self.circuit_breaker_threshold:
                self.circuit_open = True
                self.circuit_open_until = datetime.utcnow() + timedelta(seconds=self.circuit_reset_timeout)
            return False
    
    async def delete(self, key: str) -> bool:
        """Delete com circuit breaker"""
        if self.circuit_open:
            return False
        
        try:
            await self.redis.delete(key)
            return True
        except Exception:
            return False
    
    async def get_or_set(self, key: str, fetch_func: Callable, expire: int = 300) -> Any:
        """Get ou set com fallback para fetch_func se cache falhar"""
        try:
            cached = await self.get(key)
            if cached is not None:
                metrics.increment_cache_hit()
                return cached
        except Exception:
            pass  # Cache falhou, continuar com fetch
        
        metrics.increment_cache_miss()
        result = await fetch_func()
        
        # Tentar cache em background sem bloquear
        asyncio.create_task(self._set_async(key, result, expire))
        
        return result
    
    async def _set_async(self, key: str, value: Any, expire: int):
        """Set assíncrono para não bloquear resposta"""
        try:
            await self.set(key, value, expire)
        except Exception:
            pass  # Ignorar erros em background task

class CacheManager:
    """Gerenciador de cache com namespaces e invalidação inteligente"""
    
    def __init__(self, redis_client):
        self.cache = RedisCache(redis_client)
        self.hit_count = 0
        self.miss_count = 0
    
    def generate_key(self, namespace: str, *args, **kwargs) -> str:
        """Gera chave de cache consistente"""
        key_parts = [namespace]
        
        for arg in args:
            key_parts.append(str(arg))
        
        for k, v in sorted(kwargs.items()):
            key_parts.append(f"{k}:{v}")
        
        key_string = ":".join(key_parts)
        return f"cache:{hashlib.md5(key_string.encode()).hexdigest()}"
    
    async def cached(
        self, 
        namespace: str, 
        expire: int = 300,
        invalidate_on: Optional[List[str]] = None
    ):
        """Decorator para cache automático"""
        def decorator(func):
            @wraps(func)
            async def wrapper(*args, **kwargs):
                # Gerar chave baseada nos argumentos
                cache_key = self.generate_key(namespace, *args, **kwargs)
                
                # Verificar cache
                try:
                    cached_result = await self.cache.get(cache_key)
                    if cached_result is not None:
                        self.hit_count += 1
                        return cached_result
                except Exception:
                    pass  # Cache falhou, continuar
                
                self.miss_count += 1
                
                # Executar função
                result = await func(*args, **kwargs)
                
                # Cache resultado
                try:
                    await self.cache.set(cache_key, result, expire)
                except Exception:
                    pass  # Ignorar falha de cache
                
                return result
            return wrapper
        return decorator
    
    async def invalidate_namespace(self, namespace: str):
        """Invalidar todas as chaves de um namespace"""
        pattern = f"cache:*{hashlib.md5(namespace.encode()).hexdigest()[0:8]}*"
        try:
            keys = await self.cache.redis.keys(pattern)
            if keys:
                await self.cache.redis.delete(*keys)
        except Exception:
            pass
    
    async def get_hit_rate(self) -> float:
        """Calcular taxa de acerto do cache"""
        total = self.hit_count + self.miss_count
        return self.hit_count / total if total > 0 else 0.0

# api/rest/v1/endpoints/users.py - Endpoint REST otimizado
from fastapi import APIRouter, Depends, Query, Path
from sqlalchemy import select, func
from sqlalchemy.orm import selectinload, joinedload
import asyncpg

from core.database import get_db
from models.user import User
from schemas.user_schemas import UserResponse, UserListResponse, UserCreate, UserUpdate
from services.user_service import UserService
from api.middleware.auth import get_current_user
from core.cache import CacheManager

router = APIRouter()

@router.get("/users", response_model=UserListResponse)
async def list_users(
    page: int = Query(1, ge=1),
    per_page: int = Query(20, ge=1, le=100),
    search: Optional[str] = None,
    db: AsyncSession = Depends(get_db),
    cache_manager: CacheManager = Depends(lambda: app.state.cache_manager),
    current_user: User = Depends(get_current_user)
):
    """
    Listar usuários com paginação e cache
    
    Performance: 
    - Cache em Redis por 60 segundos
    - Paginação no banco (keyset pagination para grandes datasets)
    - Index covering queries
    """
    # Gerar chave de cache baseada nos parâmetros
    cache_key = cache_manager.generate_key(
        "users_list",
        page=page,
        per_page=per_page,
        search=search,
        user_id=current_user.id
    )
    
    # Tentar cache primeiro
    try:
        cached = await cache_manager.cache.get(cache_key)
        if cached:
            return

# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Pipeline de Dados em Tempo Real

## 1. Docker Compose - Infraestrutura Completa

**docker-compose.yml**
```yaml
version: '3.8'

services:
  # Kafka Cluster
  zookeeper:
    image: confluentinc/cp-zookeeper:7.4.0
    container_name: zookeeper
    environment:
      ZOOKEEPER_CLIENT_PORT: 2181
      ZOOKEEPER_TICK_TIME: 2000
    ports:
      - "2181:2181"
    networks:
      - data-network

  kafka:
    image: confluentinc/cp-kafka:7.4.0
    container_name: kafka
    depends_on:
      - zookeeper
    ports:
      - "9092:9092"
      - "29092:29092"
    environment:
      KAFKA_BROKER_ID: 1
      KAFKA_ZOOKEEPER_CONNECT: zookeeper:2181
      KAFKA_ADVERTISED_LISTENERS: PLAINTEXT://kafka:9092,PLAINTEXT_HOST://localhost:29092
      KAFKA_LISTENER_SECURITY_PROTOCOL_MAP: PLAINTEXT:PLAINTEXT,PLAINTEXT_HOST:PLAINTEXT
      KAFKA_INTER_BROKER_LISTENER_NAME: PLAINTEXT
      KAFKA_OFFSETS_TOPIC_REPLICATION_FACTOR: 1
      KAFKA_TRANSACTION_STATE_LOG_MIN_ISR: 1
      KAFKA_TRANSACTION_STATE_LOG_REPLICATION_FACTOR: 1
      KAFKA_LOG_RETENTION_HOURS: 168
      KAFKA_LOG_RETENTION_BYTES: 1073741824
    networks:
      - data-network

  # Data Warehouse
  postgres:
    image: postgres:15-alpine
    container_name: postgres-dw
    environment:
      POSTGRES_DB: diyapp_datawarehouse
      POSTGRES_USER: data_engineer
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: secure_password_123
    ports:
      - "5432:5432"
    volumes:
      - postgres_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
      - ./scripts/init_database.sql:/docker-entrypoint-initdb.d/init.sql
    networks:
      - data-network

  # Redis para cache e sessões
  redis:
    image: redis:7-alpine
    container_name: redis-cache
    ports:
      - "6379:6379"
    networks:
      - data-network

  # API Backend
  api:
    build: ./api
    container_name: data-api
    ports:
      - "8000:8000"
    environment:
      - DATABASE_URL=postgresql://data_engineer:secure_password_123@postgres:5432/diyapp_datawarehouse
      - KAFKA_BOOTSTRAP_SERVERS=kafka:9092
      - REDIS_URL=redis://redis:6379
    depends_on:
      - postgres
      - kafka
      - redis
    volumes:
      - ./api:/app
    networks:
      - data-network
    command: uvicorn app:app --host 0.0.0.0 --port 8000 --reload

  # Dashboard Frontend
  dashboard:
    build: ./dashboard
    container_name: metrics-dashboard
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
    depends_on:
      - api
    networks:
      - data-network

  # Streaming Consumers
  kafka-consumer:
    build: ./streaming/consumer
    container_name: kafka-consumer
    environment:
      - DATABASE_URL=postgresql://data_engineer:secure_password_123@postgres:5432/diyapp_datawarehouse
      - KAFKA_BOOTSTRAP_SERVERS=kafka:9092
    depends_on:
      - postgres
      - kafka
    networks:
      - data-network
    restart: unless-stopped

  # Monitoring (Grafana + Prometheus)
  prometheus:
    image: prom/prometheus:latest
    container_name: prometheus
    ports:
      - "9090:9090"
    volumes:
      - ./monitoring/prometheus.yml:/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml
    networks:
      - data-network

  grafana:
    image: grafana/grafana:latest
    container_name: grafana
    ports:
      - "3001:3000"
    environment:
      - GF_SECURITY_ADMIN_PASSWORD=admin123
    volumes:
      - ./monitoring/grafana/dashboards:/var/lib/grafana/dashboards
      - ./monitoring/grafana/provisioning:/etc/grafana/provisioning
    depends_on:
      - prometheus
    networks:
      - data-network

networks:
  data-network:
    driver: bridge

volumes:
  postgres_data:
  kafka_data:
```

## 2. Script de Inicialização do Banco de Dados

**scripts/init_database.sql**
```sql
-- Data Warehouse Schema for DIYAPP V11

-- Raw layer tables (bronze)
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS raw_app_events (
    event_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    event_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    user_id VARCHAR(100),
    session_id VARCHAR(100),
    event_timestamp TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    event_data JSONB,
    app_version VARCHAR(20),
    device_info JSONB,
    ip_address INET,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    source_topic VARCHAR(100)
);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS raw_user_actions (
    action_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    user_id VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    action_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    action_data JSONB,
    page_url VARCHAR(500),
    referrer VARCHAR(500),
    user_agent TEXT,
    timestamp TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    session_duration INTEGER,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS raw_system_logs (
    log_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    log_level VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,
    service_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    message TEXT NOT NULL,
    context JSONB,
    timestamp TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    hostname VARCHAR(100),
    trace_id VARCHAR(100),
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS raw_llm_calls (
    call_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    model_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    provider VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    prompt_tokens INTEGER,
    completion_tokens INTEGER,
    total_tokens INTEGER,
    cost_usd DECIMAL(10,6),
    latency_ms INTEGER,
    success BOOLEAN,
    error_message TEXT,
    user_id VARCHAR(100),
    feature_name VARCHAR(100),
    timestamp TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    request_metadata JSONB,
    response_metadata JSONB,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- Staging layer tables (silver)
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS stg_app_events (
    event_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    event_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    user_id VARCHAR(100),
    session_id VARCHAR(100),
    event_date DATE NOT NULL,
    event_hour INTEGER NOT NULL,
    event_timestamp TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    event_category VARCHAR(50),
    event_value DECIMAL(10,2),
    app_version VARCHAR(20),
    device_type VARCHAR(50),
    os_version VARCHAR(50),
    country_code VARCHAR(2),
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
    processed_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS stg_user_sessions (
    session_id VARCHAR(100) PRIMARY KEY,
    user_id VARCHAR(100),
    session_start TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    session_end TIMESTAMP,
    session_duration INTEGER,
    page_views INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    actions_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    device_type VARCHAR(50),
    entry_page VARCHAR(500),
    exit_page VARCHAR(500),
    bounce BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    converted BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    processed_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- Mart layer tables (gold)
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS mart_daily_metrics (
    metric_date DATE PRIMARY KEY,
    daily_active_users INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    new_users INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    returning_users INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    total_sessions INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    avg_session_duration INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    bounce_rate DECIMAL(5,2) DEFAULT 0,
    conversion_rate DECIMAL(5,2) DEFAULT 0,
    total_events INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    error_rate DECIMAL(5,2) DEFAULT 0,
    avg_response_time DECIMAL(10,2) DEFAULT 0,
    revenue DECIMAL(15,2) DEFAULT 0,
    llm_cost_total DECIMAL(15,6) DEFAULT 0,
    llm_calls_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS mart_user_behavior (
    user_id VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    behavior_date DATE NOT NULL,
    session_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    total_duration INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    pages_visited INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    actions_taken INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    conversion_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    revenue_generated DECIMAL(15,2) DEFAULT 0,
    llm_calls_made INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    favorite_features JSONB,
    user_segment VARCHAR(50),
    PRIMARY KEY (user_id, behavior_date)
);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS mart_system_health (
    check_timestamp TIMESTAMP PRIMARY KEY,
    service_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    uptime_percentage DECIMAL(5,2) DEFAULT 100.00,
    error_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    avg_latency_ms DECIMAL(10,2) DEFAULT 0,
    p95_latency_ms DECIMAL(10,2) DEFAULT 0,
    p99_latency_ms DECIMAL(10,2) DEFAULT 0,
    request_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    success_rate DECIMAL(5,2) DEFAULT 100.00,
    cpu_usage DECIMAL(5,2) DEFAULT 0,
    memory_usage DECIMAL(5,2) DEFAULT 0,
    disk_usage DECIMAL(5,2) DEFAULT 0
);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS mart_llm_cost_analysis (
    analysis_date DATE NOT NULL,
    model_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    provider VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    feature_name VARCHAR(100),
    total_calls INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    total_tokens INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    prompt_tokens INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    completion_tokens INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    total_cost_usd DECIMAL(15,6) DEFAULT 0,
    avg_latency_ms DECIMAL(10,2) DEFAULT 0,
    success_rate DECIMAL(5,2) DEFAULT 100.00,
    error_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    PRIMARY KEY (analysis_date, model_name, provider, feature_name)
);

-- Data Quality Monitoring
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS data_quality_alerts (
    alert_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    alert_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    table_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    metric_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    metric_value DECIMAL(20,6),
    threshold_value DECIMAL(20,6),
    severity VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,
    alert_message TEXT NOT NULL,
    alert_timestamp TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    resolved BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    resolved_at TIMESTAMP,
    resolution_notes TEXT
);

-- Indexes for performance
CREATE INDEX idx_raw_events_timestamp ON raw_app_events(event_timestamp);
CREATE INDEX idx_raw_events_user ON raw_app_events(user_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_stg_events_date ON stg_app_events(event_date);
CREATE INDEX idx_stg_sessions_user ON stg_user_sessions(user_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_mart_daily_metrics_date ON mart_daily_metrics(metric_date);
CREATE INDEX idx_llm_calls_timestamp ON raw_llm_calls(timestamp);
CREATE INDEX idx_llm_calls_feature ON raw_llm_calls(feature_name);

-- Create views for common queries
CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW vw_realtime_metrics AS
SELECT 
    DATE_TRUNC('minute', event_timestamp) as minute_window,
    COUNT(*) as events_per_minute,
    COUNT(DISTINCT user_id) as active_users_per_minute,
    COUNT(DISTINCT session_id) as sessions_per_minute
FROM stg_app_events 
WHERE event_timestamp > NOW() - INTERVAL '1 hour'
GROUP BY DATE_TRUNC('minute', event_timestamp)
ORDER BY minute_window DESC;

CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW vw_llm_cost_daily AS
SELECT 
    DATE(timestamp) as cost_date,
    model_name,
    provider,
    SUM(cost_usd) as daily_cost,
    COUNT(*) as total_calls,
    AVG(latency_ms) as avg_latency,
    SUM(CASE WHEN success THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) * 100.0 / COUNT(*) as success_rate
FROM raw_llm_calls
GROUP BY DATE(timestamp), model_name, provider
ORDER BY cost_date DESC;
```

## 3. Produtor Kafka para Logs em Tempo Real

**streaming/producer/app_log_producer.py**
```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Kafka Producer for DIYAPP V11 real-time logs and events
"""

import json
import time
import uuid
import random
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from typing import Dict, Any
from confluent_kafka import Producer
import logging
import sys
import os

# Configure logging
logging.basicConfig(
    level=logging.INFO,
    format='%(asctime)s - %(name)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s',
    handlers=[
        logging.FileHandler('producer.log'),
        logging.StreamHandler(sys.stdout)
    ]
)
logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

class DIYAPPKafkaProducer:
    def __init__(self, bootstrap_servers='localhost:29092'):
        """Initialize Kafka producer"""
        self.conf = {
            'bootstrap.servers': bootstrap_servers,
            'client.id': 'diyapp-producer-v11',
            'acks': 'all',
            'retries': 3,
            'compression.type': 'snappy',
            'batch.size': 16384,
            'linger.ms': 5,
            'queue.buffering.max.messages': 100000
        }
        
        self.producer = Producer(self.conf)
        self.topics = {
            'app_events': 'diyapp.app.events',
            'user_actions': 'diyapp.user.actions',
            'system_logs': 'diyapp.system.logs',
            'llm_calls': 'diyapp.llm.calls',
            'data_quality': 'diyapp.data.quality'
        }
        
        logger.info(f"Initialized producer for topics: {list(self.topics.values())}")
    
    def delivery_report(self, err, msg):
        """Callback for message delivery reports"""
        if err is not None:
            logger.error(f'Message delivery failed: {err}')
        else:
            logger.debug(f'Message delivered to {msg.topic()} [{msg.partition()}]')
    
    def produce_app_event(self, event_type: str, user_id: str = None, 
                         session_id: str = None, **kwargs):
        """Produce application event"""
        event = {
            'event_id': str(uuid.uuid4()),
            'event_type': event_type,
            'user_id': user_id or f"user_{random.randint(1000, 9999)}",
            '

### [Sessão Paralela: SRE]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Infraestrutura como Código

Vou criar uma infraestrutura Kubernetes completa com auto-scaling, service mesh (Istio) para observabilidade e plano de disaster recovery. Organizarei em uma estrutura profissional com templates Helm, configurações de auto-scaling e implementação de Istio.

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-v11-infra/
├── README.md
├── kubernetes/
│   ├── base/
│   │   ├── kustomization.yaml
│   │   ├── namespace.yaml
│   │   ├── configs/
│   │   └── secrets/
│   ├── overlays/
│   │   ├── development/
│   │   ├── staging/
│   │   └── production/
│   └── crds/

## 1. Templates Helm para DIYAPP

### `helm/diyapp/Chart.yaml`
```yaml
apiVersion: v2
name: diyapp
description: DIYAPP Evolution V11 - Core Application
type: application
version: 11.0.0
appVersion: "11.0.0"
dependencies:
  - name: redis
    version: 17.11.0
    repository: https://charts.bitnami.com/bitnami
    condition: redis.enabled
  - name: postgresql
    version: 12.9.0
    repository: https://charts.bitnami.com/bitnami
    condition: postgresql.enabled
```

### `helm/diyapp/values.yaml`
```yaml
# Global values
global:
  environment: production
  region: us-east-1
  clusterName: diyapp-v11

# Application configuration
app:
  name: diyapp
  version: "11.0.0"
  replicaCount: 3
  revisionHistoryLimit: 10
  
  image:
    repository: registry.diyapp.io/diyapp-v11
    tag: latest
    pullPolicy: IfNotPresent
    pullSecrets:
      - name: registry-credentials

  resources:
    requests:
      memory: "512Mi"
      cpu: "250m"
    limits:
      memory: "1024Mi"
      cpu: "500m"

  # SLO-based configuration
  slo:
    availability: 99.9
    latencyP95: 300
    errorRate: 0.1
    llmLatencyP95: 8000

  # Health checks
  livenessProbe:
    httpGet:
      path: /health/liveness
      port: 8080
    initialDelaySeconds: 30
    periodSeconds: 10
    timeoutSeconds: 5
    failureThreshold: 3

  readinessProbe:
    httpGet:
      path: /health/readiness
      port: 8080
    initialDelaySeconds: 5
    periodSeconds: 5
    timeoutSeconds: 3
    failureThreshold: 3

  # Auto-scaling configuration
  autoscaling:
    enabled: true
    minReplicas: 3
    maxReplicas: 20
    targetCPUUtilizationPercentage: 70
    targetMemoryUtilizationPercentage: 80
    behavior:
      scaleDown:
        stabilizationWindowSeconds: 300
        policies:
        - type: Percent
          value: 10
          periodSeconds: 60
      scaleUp:
        stabilizationWindowSeconds: 60
        policies:
        - type: Percent
          value: 100
          periodSeconds: 60

# Service configuration
service:
  type: ClusterIP
  port: 8080
  targetPort: 8080
  annotations:
    prometheus.io/scrape: "true"
    prometheus.io/port: "8080"
    prometheus.io/path: "/metrics"

# Ingress configuration
ingress:
  enabled: true
  className: istio
  annotations:
    kubernetes.io/ingress.class: istio
    cert-manager.io/cluster-issuer: "letsencrypt-prod"
  hosts:
    - host: app.diyapp.io
      paths:
        - path: /
          pathType: Prefix
  tls:
    - secretName: diyapp-tls
      hosts:
        - app.diyapp.io

# Database configuration
postgresql:
  enabled: true
  architecture: replication
  auth:
    database: diyapp
    username: diyapp
    password: ""
  primary:
    persistence:
      size: 100Gi
      storageClass: gp3
    resources:
      requests:
        memory: 4Gi
        cpu: 2
  readReplicas:
    replicaCount: 2
    persistence:
      size: 100Gi
      storageClass: gp3

# Redis configuration
redis:
  enabled: true
  architecture: replication
  auth:
    password: ""
  master:
    persistence:
      size: 50Gi
      storageClass: gp3
    resources:
      requests:
        memory: 4Gi
        cpu: 2
  replica:
    replicaCount: 2
    persistence:
      size: 50Gi

# Monitoring configuration
monitoring:
  enabled: true
  prometheus:
    scrapeInterval: 30s
  grafana:
    enabled: true
  alerts:
    enabled: true

# Istio configuration
istio:
  enabled: true
  sidecarInject: true
  mtls:
    mode: STRICT
  traffic:
    canary:
      enabled: false
      weight: 10

# Disaster Recovery configuration
disasterRecovery:
  enabled: true
  backup:
    schedule: "0 2 * * *"
    retentionDays: 30
  rpo: 300  # 5 minutes in seconds
  rto: 900  # 15 minutes in seconds
```

### `helm/diyapp/templates/deployment.yaml`
```yaml
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  name: {{ include "diyapp.fullname" . }}
  namespace: {{ .Release.Namespace }}
  labels:
    {{- include "diyapp.labels" . | nindent 4 }}
    app.kubernetes.io/component: api
  annotations:
    rollme: {{ randAlphaNum 5 | quote }}
    {{- if .Values.app.slo }}
    slo.availability: {{ .Values.app.slo.availability | quote }}
    slo.latencyP95: {{ .Values.app.slo.latencyP95 | quote }}
    slo.errorRate: {{ .Values.app.slo.errorRate | quote }}
    {{- end }}
spec:
  replicas: {{ .Values.app.replicaCount }}
  revisionHistoryLimit: {{ .Values.app.revisionHistoryLimit }}
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      {{- include "diyapp.selectorLabels" . | nindent 6 }}
  strategy:
    type: RollingUpdate
    rollingUpdate:
      maxSurge: 25%
      maxUnavailable: 25%
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        {{- include "diyapp.labels" . | nindent 8 }}
        app.kubernetes.io/component: api
        version: {{ .Values.app.version | quote }}
      annotations:
        checksum/config: {{ include (print $.Template.BasePath "/configmap.yaml") . | sha256sum }}
        prometheus.io/scrape: "true"
        prometheus.io/port: "8080"
        prometheus.io/path: "/metrics"
        {{- if .Values.istio.enabled }}
        sidecar.istio.io/inject: "{{ .Values.istio.sidecarInject }}"
        {{- end }}
    spec:
      {{- if .Values.app.image.pullSecrets }}
      imagePullSecrets:
        {{- toYaml .Values.app.image.pullSecrets | nindent 8 }}
      {{- end }}
      serviceAccountName: {{ include "diyapp.serviceAccountName" . }}
      securityContext:
        fsGroup: 1000
        runAsUser: 1000
        runAsNonRoot: true
      containers:
      - name: {{ .Chart.Name }}
        image: "{{ .Values.app.image.repository }}:{{ .Values.app.image.tag | default .Chart.AppVersion }}"
        imagePullPolicy: {{ .Values.app.image.pullPolicy }}
        ports:
        - name: http
          containerPort: 8080
          protocol: TCP
        - name: metrics
          containerPort: 9090
          protocol: TCP
        env:
        - name: NODE_ENV
          value: {{ .Values.global.environment | quote }}
        - name: POD_NAME
          valueFrom:
            fieldRef:
              fieldPath: metadata.name
        - name: POD_NAMESPACE
          valueFrom:
            fieldRef:
              fieldPath: metadata.namespace
        - name: POD_IP
          valueFrom:
            fieldRef:
              fieldPath: status.podIP
        envFrom:
        - configMapRef:
            name: {{ include "diyapp.fullname" . }}-config
        - secretRef:
            name: {{ include "diyapp.fullname" . }}-secrets
        resources:
          {{- toYaml .Values.app.resources | nindent 12 }}
        livenessProbe:
          {{- toYaml .Values.app.livenessProbe | nindent 12 }}
        readinessProbe:
          {{- toYaml .Values.app.readinessProbe | nindent 12 }}
        volumeMounts:
        - name: config-volume
          mountPath: /app/config
        - name: tmp-volume
          mountPath: /tmp
        securityContext:
          allowPrivilegeEscalation: false
          readOnlyRootFilesystem: true
          capabilities:
            drop:
            - ALL
      volumes:
      - name: config-volume
        configMap:
          name: {{ include "diyapp.fullname" . }}-config
      - name: tmp-volume
        emptyDir: {}
      {{- if .Values.istio.enabled }}
      - name: istio-token
        projected:
          sources:
          - serviceAccountToken:
              audience: istio-ca
              expirationSeconds: 43200
              path: istio-token
      {{- end }}
      affinity:
        podAntiAffinity:
          preferredDuringSchedulingIgnoredDuringExecution:
          - weight: 100
            podAffinityTerm:
              labelSelector:
                matchExpressions:
                - key: app.kubernetes.io/name
                  operator: In
                  values:
                  - {{ include "diyapp.name" . }}
              topologyKey: kubernetes.io/hostname
        nodeAffinity:
          preferredDuringSchedulingIgnoredDuringExecution:
          - weight: 1
            preference:
              matchExpressions:
              - key: node-type
                operator: In
                values:
                - application
```

### `helm/diyapp/templates/hpa.yaml`
```yaml
{{- if .Values.app.autoscaling.enabled }}
apiVersion: autoscaling/v2
kind: HorizontalPodAutoscaler
metadata:
  name: {{ include "diyapp.fullname" . }}-hpa
  namespace: {{ .Release.Namespace }}
  labels:
    {{- include "diyapp.labels" . | nindent 4 }}
spec:
  scaleTargetRef:
    apiVersion: apps/v1
    kind: Deployment
    name: {{ include "diyapp.fullname" . }}
  minReplicas: {{ .Values.app.autoscaling.minReplicas }}
  maxReplicas: {{ .Values.app.autoscaling.maxReplicas }}
  metrics:
  - type: Resource
    resource:
      name: cpu
      target:
        type: Utilization
        averageUtilization: {{ .Values.app.autoscaling.targetCPUUtilizationPercentage }}
  - type: Resource
    resource:
      name: memory
      target:
        type: Utilization
        averageUtilization: {{ .Values.app.autoscaling.targetMemoryUtilizationPercentage }}
  - type: Pods
    pods:
      metric:
        name: http_requests_per_second
      target:
        type: AverageValue
        averageValue: 100
  behavior:
    scaleDown:
      stabilizationWindowSeconds: {{ .Values.app.autoscaling.behavior.scaleDown.stabilizationWindowSeconds }}
      policies:
      {{- toYaml .Values.app.autoscaling.behavior.scaleDown.policies | nindent 6 }}
    scaleUp:
      stabilizationWindowSeconds: {{ .Values.app.autoscaling.behavior.scaleUp.stabilizationWindowSeconds }}
      policies:
      {{- toYaml .Values.app.autoscaling.behavior.scaleUp.policies | nindent 6 }}
{{- end }}
```

### `helm/diyapp/templates/pdb.yaml`
```yaml
apiVersion: policy/v1
kind: PodDisruptionBudget
metadata:
  name: {{ include "diyapp.fullname" . }}-pdb
  namespace: {{ .Release.Namespace }}
  labels:
    {{- include "diyapp.labels" . | nindent 4 }}
spec:
  minAvailable: 50%
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      {{- include "diyapp.selectorLabels" . | nindent 6 }}
```

## 2. Configuração de Istio para Observabilidade

### `istio/gateway.yaml`
```yaml
apiVersion: networking.istio.io/v1beta1
kind: Gateway
metadata:
  name: diyapp-gateway
  namespace: diyapp
spec:
  selector:
    istio: ingressgateway
  servers:
  - port:
      number: 80
      name: http
      protocol: HTTP
    hosts:
    - "app.diyapp.io"
    - "*.diyapp.io"
    tls:
      httpsRedirect: true
  - port:
      number: 443
      name: https
      protocol: HTTPS
    hosts:
    - "app.diyapp.io"
    - "*.diyapp.io"
    tls:
      mode: SIMPLE
      credentialName: diyapp-tls
```

### `istio/virtualservice.yaml`
```yaml
apiVersion: networking.istio.io/v1beta1
kind: VirtualService
metadata:
  name: diyapp-vs
  namespace: diyapp
spec:
  hosts:
  - "app.diyapp.io"
  - "api.diyapp.io"
  gateways:
  - diyapp-gateway
  http:
  - name: "main-route"
    match:
    - uri:
        prefix: "/"
    route:
    - destination:
        host: diyapp-service.diyapp.svc.cluster.local
        port:
          number: 8080
      weight: 100
    timeout: 30s
    retries:
      attempts: 3
      perTryTimeout: 2s
      retryOn: gateway-error,connect-failure,refused-stream
    corsPolicy:
      allowOrigins:
      - exact: "https://app.diyapp.io"
      allowMethods:
      - GET
      - POST
      - PUT
      - DELETE
      - OPTIONS
      allowHeaders:
      - content-type
      - authorization
      - x-request-id
      - x-b3-traceid
      - x-b3-spanid
      - x-b3-parentspanid
      - x-b3-sampled
      - x-b3-flags
      - x-ot-span-context
    fault:
      delay:
        percentage:
          value: 0.1
        fixedDelay: 5s
  - name: "health-route"
    match:
    - uri:
        exact: "/health"
    - uri:
        exact: "/health/readiness"
    - uri:
        exact: "/health/liveness"
    route:
    - destination:
        host: diyapp-service.diyapp.svc.cluster.local
        port:
          number: 8080
    timeout: 5s
```

### `istio/destinationrule.yaml`
```yaml
apiVersion: networking.istio.io/v1beta1
kind: DestinationRule
metadata:
  name: diyapp-dr
  namespace: diyapp
spec:
  host: diyapp-service.diyapp.svc.cluster.local
  trafficPolicy:
    connectionPool:
      tcp:
        maxConnections: 100
        connectTimeout: 30ms
      http:
        http1MaxPendingRequests: 50
        http2MaxRequests: 100
        maxRequestsPerConnection: 10
        maxRetries: 3
    outlierDetection:
      consecutive5xxErrors: 5
      interval: 30s
      baseEjectionTime: 30s
      maxEjectionPercent: 50
    tls:
      mode: ISTIO_MUTUAL
  subsets:
  - name: v1
    labels:
      version: "11.0.0"
    trafficPolicy:
      loadBalancer:

### [Sessão Paralela: Segurança]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Hardening de Segurança

Vou implementar um hardening completo de segurança com foco nos pontos críticos identificados. Usarei o framework STRIDE para garantir cobertura completa.

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-v11-security/
├── src/
│   ├── security/
│   │   ├── auth/
│   │   │   ├── oauth2.1.js
│   │   │   ├── jwt-rotation.js
│   │   │   └── mfa.js
│   │   ├── encryption/
│   │   │   ├── at-rest.js
│   │   │   ├── in-transit.js
│   │   │   └── key-management.js
│   │   ├── waf/
│   │   │   ├── rules.js
│   │   │   └── middleware.js
│   │   ├── scanning/
│   │   │   ├── dependency-scanner.js
│   │   │   └── vulnerability-monitor.js
│   │   └── audit/
│   │       ├── logger.js
│   │       └── compliance.js
│   ├── middleware/
│   │   ├── security-headers.js
│   │   └── rate-limiter.js
│   └── app.js
├── public/
│   └── index.html
├── tests/
│   └── security.test.js
├── package.json
├── docker-compose.yml
├── .snyk
├── .env.example
└── README.md
```

## 1. Configuração Principal de Segurança

### `src/app.js` - Ponto de entrada com todas as proteções
```javascript
const express = require('express');
const helmet = require('helmet');
const cors = require('cors');
const rateLimit = require('express-rate-limit');
const { v4: uuidv4 } = require('uuid');

// Importações de segurança
const securityHeaders = require('./middleware/security-headers');
const wafMiddleware = require('./security/waf/middleware');
const dependencyScanner = require('./security/scanning/dependency-scanner');
const auditLogger = require('./security/audit/logger');

// Inicialização do scanner de dependências
dependencyScanner.initialize();

const app = express();

// 1. Helmet para headers de segurança
app.use(helmet({
  contentSecurityPolicy: {
    directives: {
      defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
      styleSrc: ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'"],
      scriptSrc: ["'self'"],
      imgSrc: ["'self'", "data:", "https:"],
      connectSrc: ["'self'"],
      fontSrc: ["'self'"],
      objectSrc: ["'none'"],
      mediaSrc: ["'self'"],
      frameSrc: ["'none'"],
    },
  },
  hsts: {
    maxAge: 31536000,
    includeSubDomains: true,
    preload: true
  },
  referrerPolicy: { policy: 'strict-origin-when-cross-origin' }
}));

// 2. CORS seguro
app.use(cors({
  origin: process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGINS ? process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGINS.split(',') : ['https://app.diyapp.com'],
  credentials: true,
  methods: ['GET', 'POST', 'PUT', 'DELETE', 'OPTIONS'],
  allowedHeaders: ['Content-Type', 'Authorization', 'X-Request-ID'],
  maxAge: 86400
}));

// 3. Rate limiting por tipo de endpoint
const apiLimiter = rateLimit({
  windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutos
  max: 100, // limite por IP
  message: 'Too many requests from this IP, please try again later.',
  standardHeaders: true,
  legacyHeaders: false,
  keyGenerator: (req) => {
    return req.ip + (req.user ? req.user.id : '');
  }
});

const authLimiter = rateLimit({
  windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000,
  max: 5, // Apenas 5 tentativas de login
  message: 'Too many login attempts, please try again later.',
  skipSuccessfulRequests: true
});

// 4. WAF - Web Application Firewall
app.use(wafMiddleware);

// 5. Headers de segurança customizados
app.use(securityHeaders);

// 6. Request ID para rastreabilidade
app.use((req, res, next) => {
  req.requestId = uuidv4();
  res.setHeader('X-Request-ID', req.requestId);
  next();
});

// 7. Logging de auditoria
app.use(auditLogger.requestLogger);

// Aplicar rate limiting
app.use('/api/auth/', authLimiter);
app.use('/api/', apiLimiter);

// Body parsers com limites
app.use(express.json({ limit: '10kb' }));
app.use(express.urlencoded({ extended: true, limit: '10kb' }));

// Rotas principais
app.use('/api/auth', require('./routes/auth'));
app.use('/api/users', require('./routes/users'));
app.use('/api/data', require('./routes/data'));

// Health check com verificação de segurança
app.get('/health', (req, res) => {
  const securityStatus = dependencyScanner.getSecurityStatus();
  
  res.json({
    status: 'ok',
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
    security: {
      dependencies: securityStatus.dependencies,
      vulnerabilities: securityStatus.vulnerabilities,
      lastScan: securityStatus.lastScan
    },
    uptime: process.uptime()
  });
});

// Error handling seguro
app.use((err, req, res, next) => {
  auditLogger.securityEvent('ERROR', {
    requestId: req.requestId,
    path: req.path,
    method: req.method,
    error: err.message,
    stack: process.env.NODE_ENV === 'development' ? err.stack : undefined,
    userId: req.user ? req.user.id : 'anonymous'
  });

  // Não expor detalhes do erro em produção
  const response = {
    error: 'An error occurred',
    requestId: req.requestId
  };

  if (process.env.NODE_ENV === 'development') {
    response.details = err.message;
  }

  res.status(err.status || 500).json(response);
});

// Inicialização do servidor
const PORT = process.env.PORT || 3000;
const server = app.listen(PORT, () => {
  console.log(`DIYAPP V11 Security running on port ${PORT}`);
  
  // Verificação inicial de segurança
  dependencyScanner.scanImmediate().then(result => {
    if (result.critical > 0) {
      console.error('⚠️  CRITICAL VULNERABILITIES DETECTED!');
      process.exit(1);
    }
  });
});

module.exports = { app, server };
```

## 2. OAuth 2.1 com JWT Rotation

### `src/security/auth/oauth2.1.js`
```javascript
const crypto = require('crypto');
const { Issuer } = require('openid-client');
const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');
const { promisify } = require('util');

class OAuth21Manager {
  constructor() {
    this.clients = new Map();
    this.jwksCache = new Map();
    this.tokenRotationEnabled = true;
  }

  async initializeProvider(providerConfig) {
    const {
      name,
      issuer,
      clientId,
      clientSecret,
      redirectUris,
      scopes = ['openid', 'profile', 'email']
    } = providerConfig;

    try {
      const issuerInstance = await Issuer.discover(issuer);
      
      const client = new issuerInstance.Client({
        client_id: clientId,
        client_secret: clientSecret,
        redirect_uris: redirectUris,
        response_types: ['code'],
        token_endpoint_auth_method: 'client_secret_post'
      });

      // Configuração de segurança OAuth 2.1
      client[crypto.randomUUID] = {
        pkce: true,
        state: true,
        nonce: true,
        maxAge: 3600 // 1 hora
      };

      this.clients.set(name, client);
      
      // Cache de JWKS
      await this.refreshJWKS(name, client);
      
      console.log(`✅ OAuth 2.1 provider ${name} initialized`);
      return client;
    } catch (error) {
      console.error(`❌ Failed to initialize OAuth provider ${name}:`, error);
      throw error;
    }
  }

  async refreshJWKS(name, client) {
    try {
      const jwks = await client.keystore();
      this.jwksCache.set(name, {
        jwks,
        refreshedAt: Date.now(),
        ttl: 3600000 // 1 hora
      });
    } catch (error) {
      console.error(`Failed to refresh JWKS for ${name}:`, error);
    }
  }

  async validateToken(token, providerName) {
    const client = this.clients.get(providerName);
    if (!client) {
      throw new Error(`Provider ${providerName} not found`);
    }

    // Verificar se o JWKS precisa ser atualizado
    const cached = this.jwksCache.get(providerName);
    if (!cached || Date.now() - cached.refreshedAt > cached.ttl) {
      await this.refreshJWKS(providerName, client);
    }

    try {
      const verified = await client.verifyIdToken(token);
      
      // Validações adicionais de segurança
      this.validateTokenClaims(verified);
      
      return verified;
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Token validation failed:', error);
      throw new Error('Invalid token');
    }
  }

  validateTokenClaims(claims) {
    const now = Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000);
    
    // Verificar expiração
    if (claims.exp && claims.exp < now) {
      throw new Error('Token expired');
    }
    
    // Verificar issued at
    if (claims.iat && claims.iat > now + 300) { // 5 minutos de tolerância
      throw new Error('Token issued in the future');
    }
    
    // Verificar nonce para prevenir replay attacks
    if (!claims.nonce) {
      throw new Error('Missing nonce claim');
    }
    
    // Verificar audience
    if (claims.aud !== process.env.OAUTH_CLIENT_ID) {
      throw new Error('Invalid audience');
    }
  }

  async generateAuthUrl(providerName, options = {}) {
    const client = this.clients.get(providerName);
    if (!client) {
      throw new Error(`Provider ${providerName} not found`);
    }

    const {
      redirectUri,
      scope = ['openid', 'profile', 'email'],
      state,
      nonce
    } = options;

    // Gerar PKCE code verifier e challenge
    const codeVerifier = crypto.randomBytes(32).toString('base64url');
    const codeChallenge = crypto
      .createHash('sha256')
      .update(codeVerifier)
      .digest('base64url');

    const params = {
      redirect_uri: redirectUri,
      scope: scope.join(' '),
      state: state || crypto.randomBytes(16).toString('hex'),
      nonce: nonce || crypto.randomBytes(16).toString('hex'),
      code_challenge: codeChallenge,
      code_challenge_method: 'S256',
      response_type: 'code',
      prompt: 'consent',
      access_type: 'offline'
    };

    const authUrl = client.authorizationUrl(params);
    
    return {
      url: authUrl,
      codeVerifier,
      state: params.state,
      nonce: params.nonce
    };
  }

  async exchangeCode(code, providerName, codeVerifier, redirectUri) {
    const client = this.clients.get(providerName);
    if (!client) {
      throw new Error(`Provider ${providerName} not found`);
    }

    const params = {
      code,
      redirect_uri: redirectUri,
      code_verifier: codeVerifier
    };

    try {
      const tokenSet = await client.callback(redirectUri, params, {
        state: params.state,
        nonce: params.nonce
      });

      // Rotação automática de refresh tokens
      if (this.tokenRotationEnabled && tokenSet.refresh_token) {
        await this.rotateRefreshToken(providerName, tokenSet.refresh_token);
      }

      return tokenSet;
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Code exchange failed:', error);
      throw new Error('Failed to exchange authorization code');
    }
  }

  async rotateRefreshToken(providerName, oldRefreshToken) {
    // Implementar lógica de rotação de refresh token
    // Invalida o token antigo e gera um novo
    console.log(`Rotating refresh token for ${providerName}`);
    
    // Em produção, registrar a invalidação no banco de dados
    await this.invalidateToken(oldRefreshToken);
  }

  async invalidateToken(token) {
    // Implementar invalidação de token
    // Registrar em blacklist ou banco de dados
    console.log('Invalidating token:', token.substring(0, 10) + '...');
  }
}

module.exports = new OAuth21Manager();
```

## 3. Sistema de Rotação de JWT

### `src/security/auth/jwt-rotation.js`
```javascript
const crypto = require('crypto');
const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');
const { promisify } = require('util');
const Redis = require('ioredis');

class JWTRotationManager {
  constructor() {
    this.redis = new Redis(process.env.REDIS_URL || 'redis://localhost:6379');
    this.keyRotationInterval = 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000; // 24 horas
    this.accessTokenTTL = 15 * 60; // 15 minutos
    this.refreshTokenTTL = 7 * 24 * 60 * 60; // 7 dias
    
    // Inicializar chaves
    this.initializeKeys();
    
    // Agendar rotação automática
    setInterval(() => this.rotateKeys(), this.keyRotationInterval);
  }

  async initializeKeys() {
    // Verificar se existem chaves no Redis
    const currentKey = await this.redis.get('jwt:current:key');
    
    if (!currentKey) {
      // Gerar novo par de chaves
      await this.generateNewKeyPair();
    }
  }

  async generateNewKeyPair() {
    // Gerar chave HMAC para assinatura
    const hmacKey = crypto.randomBytes(64).toString('hex');
    
    // Gerar chaves RSA para rotação (se necessário)
    const { publicKey, privateKey } = crypto.generateKeyPairSync('rsa', {
      modulusLength: 4096,
      publicKeyEncoding: {
        type: 'spki',
        format: 'pem'
      },
      privateKeyEncoding: {
        type: 'pkcs8',
        format: 'pem'
      }
    });

    const keyId = crypto.randomBytes(8).toString('hex');
    const timestamp = Date.now();
    
    const keyData = {
      id: keyId,
      hmacKey,
      privateKey,
      publicKey,
      createdAt: timestamp,
      active: true
    };

    // Armazenar nova chave
    await this.redis.set(`jwt:key:${keyId}`, JSON.stringify(keyData));
    
    // Atualizar chave atual
    await this.redis.set('jwt:current:key', keyId);
    
    // Manter histórico de chaves (últimas 5)
    await this.redis.lpush('jwt:key:history', keyId);
    await this.redis.ltrim('jwt:key:history', 0, 4);
    
    console.log(`✅ New JWT key pair generated: ${keyId}`);
    
    return keyId;
  }

  async rotateKeys() {
    console.log('🔄 Rotating JWT keys...');
    
    // Gerar nova chave
    const newKeyId = await this.generateNewKeyPair();
    
    // Desativar chaves antigas após período de transição
    const oldKeyId = await this.redis.get('jwt:current:key');
    if (oldKeyId && oldKeyId !== newKeyId) {
      await this.deactivateKey(oldKeyId);
    }
    
    // Limpar tokens expirados
    await this.cleanupExpiredTokens();
  }

  async deactivateKey(keyId) {
    const keyData = await this.redis.get(`jwt:key:${keyId}`);
    if (keyData) {
      const parsed = JSON.parse(keyData);
      parsed.active = false;
      parsed.deactivatedAt = Date.now();
      
      await this.redis.set(`jwt:key:${keyId}`, JSON.stringify(parsed));
      console.log(`🔒 Deactivated JWT key: ${keyId}`);
    }
  }

  async generateTokenPair(userId, payload = {}) {
    const keyId = await this.redis.get('jwt:current:key');
    const keyData = JSON.parse(await this.redis.get(`jwt:key:${keyId}`));
    
    if (!keyData || !keyData.active) {
      throw new Error('No active JWT key available');
    }

    const accessTokenPayload = {
      ...payload,
      sub: userId,
      type: 'access',
      iat: Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000),
      exp: Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000) + this.accessTokenTTL,
      jti: crypto.randomBytes(16).toString('hex'),
      kid: keyId
    };

    const refreshTokenPayload = {
      sub: userId,
      type: 'refresh',
      iat: Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000),
      exp: Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000) + this.refreshTokenTTL,
      jti: crypto.randomBytes(16).toString('hex'),
      kid: keyId
    };

    // Gerar tokens
    const accessToken = jwt.sign(
      accessTokenPayload,
      keyData.hmacKey,
      { algorithm: 'HS512' }
    );

    const refreshToken = jwt.sign(
      refreshTokenPayload,
      keyData.hmacKey,
      { algorithm

### [Sessão Paralela: QA]

## 4. Script do Dashboard (dashboard.js)

```javascript
// dashboard.js
class StabilityDashboard {
    constructor() {
        this.ws = null;
        this.charts = {};
        this.logEntries = [];
        this.autoScroll = true;
        this.initialize();
    }

    initialize() {
        this.connectWebSocket();
        this.initializeCharts();
        this.updateLastRun();
        this.startMetricsPolling();
        this.setupEventListeners();
    }

    connectWebSocket() {
        const protocol = window.location.protocol === 'https:' ? 'wss:' : 'ws:';
        const wsUrl = `${protocol}//${window.location.host}/ws`;
        
        this.ws = new WebSocket(wsUrl);
        
        this.ws.onopen = () => {
            this.addLog('🔗 Conectado ao servidor de métricas em tempo real');
        };

        this.ws.onmessage = (event) => {
            const data = JSON.parse(event.data);
            this.handleWebSocketMessage(data);
        };

        this.ws.onerror = (error) => {
            this.addLog('❌ Erro na conexão WebSocket', 'error');
            console.error('WebSocket error:', error);
        };

        this.ws.onclose = () => {
            this.addLog('🔌 Conexão WebSocket fechada. Reconectando...', 'warning');
            setTimeout(() => this.connectWebSocket(), 3000);
        };
    }

    handleWebSocketMessage(data) {
        switch(data.type) {
            case 'metrics':
                this.updateMetrics(data.payload);
                break;
            case 'test_result':
                this.handleTestResult(data.payload);
                break;
            case 'chaos_event':
                this.handleChaosEvent(data.payload);
                break;
            case 'log':
                this.addLog(data.message, data.level);
                break;
        }
    }

    initializeCharts() {
        const latencyCtx = document.getElementById('latencyChart').getContext('2d');
        this.charts.latency = new Chart(latencyCtx, {
            type: 'line',
            data: {
                labels: [],
                datasets: [{
                    label: 'Latência p95 (ms)',
                    data: [],
                    borderColor: '#3b82f6',
                    backgroundColor: 'rgba(59, 130, 246, 0.1)',
                    tension: 0.4
                }]
            },
            options: {
                responsive: true,
                plugins: {
                    legend: { display: true }
                },
                scales: {
                    y: {
                        beginAtZero: true,
                        title: {
                            display: true,
                            text: 'Milissegundos'
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        });

        const errorCtx = document.getElementById('errorChart').getContext('2d');
        this.charts.error = new Chart(errorCtx, {
            type: 'bar',
            data: {
                labels: [],
                datasets: [{
                    label: 'Taxa de Erros (%)',
                    data: [],
                    backgroundColor: '#ef4444',
                    borderColor: '#dc2626',
                    borderWidth: 1
                }]
            },
            options: {
                responsive: true,
                plugins: {
                    legend: { display: true }
                },
                scales: {
                    y: {
                        beginAtZero: true,
                        max: 100,
                        title: {
                            display: true,
                            text: 'Porcentagem'
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        });
    }

    updateMetrics(metrics) {
        // Atualizar indicadores de status
        this.updateStatusIndicator('load', metrics.loadTest);
        this.updateStatusIndicator('chaos', metrics.chaosStatus);
        this.updateStatusIndicator('visual', metrics.visualRegression);
        this.updateStatusIndicator('failover', metrics.failoverStatus);

        // Atualizar métricas textuais
        document.getElementById('load-metrics').textContent = 
            `RPS: ${metrics.rps || 0} | Erros: ${metrics.errorRate || 0}%`;
        
        document.getElementById('chaos-metrics').textContent = 
            `Injeções: ${metrics.chaosInjected || 0} | Recuperações: ${metrics.recoveries || 0}`;

        // Atualizar gráficos
        this.updateChart('latency', metrics.timestamp, metrics.p95Latency);
        this.updateChart('error', metrics.timestamp, metrics.errorRate);
    }

    updateStatusIndicator(type, status) {
        const indicator = document.getElementById(`${type}-indicator`);
        const card = document.getElementById(`${type}-status`);
        
        let color, text;
        
        switch(status) {
            case 'healthy':
                color = '#10b981';
                text =

        // Atualizar hora atual
        function updateTime() {
            const now = new Date();
            document.getElementById('current-time').textContent = 
                now.toLocaleString('pt-BR', { 
                    timeZone: 'America/Sao_Paulo',
                    hour12: false 
                });
            
            document.getElementById('last-updated').textContent = 
                now.toLocaleDateString('pt-BR') + ' ' + 
                now.toLocaleTimeString('pt-BR', { hour12: false });
        }
        
        // Inicializar
        updateTime();
        setInterval(updateTime, 60000);

            // Em implementação real, abriria o arquivo MD correspondente

        // Simular verificação de saúde do sistema
        async function checkSystemHealth() {
            try {
                const response = await fetch('/api/health', { method: 'GET' });
                if (!response.ok) {
                    document.querySelector('.status-dot').style.background = 'var(--danger)';
                }
            } catch (error) {
                console.log('Health check simulation:', error);
            }
        }
        
        // Verificar saúde periodicamente
        setInterval(checkSystemHealth, 30000);
    </script>

## 2. Runbooks para SRE

### 2.1 `/runbooks/incident-response.md`

```markdown
# Runbook: Resposta a Incidentes - DIYAPP V11

**Owner:** SRE Squad  
**Última atualização:** $(date +%Y-%m-%d)  
**Severidade:** Crítico  
**Tempo alvo de resolução:** 15 minutos

## 1. Classificação do Incidente

### 1.1 Níveis de Severidade

| Nível | Impacto | Exemplo | Ação |
|-------|---------|---------|------|
| SEV-1 | Sistema completamente inacessível | API retorna 5xx para >95% requests | Acionamento imediato da squad |
| SEV-2 | Funcionalidade crítica degradada | Latência >5s para 50% requests | Auto-cura + notificação SRE |
| SEV-3 | Funcionalidade não-crítica afetada | Feature específica com erro | Auto-cura + log para análise |
| SEV-4 | Problema menor | Logs com warnings | Monitoramento automático |

### 1.2 Gatilhos Automáticos

```yaml
# /monitoring/alerts.yaml
triggers:
  sev1:
    - api_error_rate > 95%
    - database_connections > 90%
    - service_unavailable > 5min
  sev2:
    - latency_p95 > 5000ms
    - memory_usage > 85%
    - queue_size > 1000
  sev3:
    - error_rate > 10%
    - disk_usage > 80%
    - failed_jobs > 100
```

## 2. Procedimento de Resposta

### 2

### [Sessão Paralela: Inovação]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Sistema de Feature Flags Avançado

Vou implementar um sistema completo de feature flags com rollout gradual, targeting por segmentos e analytics integrado. O sistema será 100% autônomo e pronto para produção.

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
feature-flags-system/
├── index.html              # Dashboard de administração
├── package.json
├── README.md
├── src/
│   ├── server.js          # Servidor principal
│   ├── database.js        # Configuração do banco de dados
│   ├── feature-flags.js   # Core do sistema de feature flags
│   ├── analytics.js       # Sistema de analytics integrado
│   ├── targeting.js       # Lógica de segmentação
│   ├── api/
│   │   ├── flags.js       # API REST para feature flags
│   │   ├── analytics.js   # API para analytics
│   │   └── admin.js       # API administrativa
│   ├── models/
│   │   ├── Flag.js        # Modelo de feature flag
│   │   ├── Event.js       # Modelo de eventos de analytics
│   │   └── Segment.js     # Modelo de segmentos
│   ├── middleware/
│   │   ├── auth.js        # Autenticação
│   │   └── validation.js  # Validação de requests
│   └── utils/
│       ├── logger.js      # Sistema de logging
│       └── crypto.js      # Utilitários de criptografia
├── public/
│   ├── css/
│   │   └── style.css      # Estilos do dashboard
│   └── js/
│       └── dashboard.js   # JavaScript do dashboard
├── tests/
│   ├── feature-flags.test.js
│   └── analytics.test.js
└── config/
    └── default.json       # Configurações
```
