## 1. Core - FeatureFlagManager.js

```javascript
// src/core/FeatureFlagManager.js
const EventEmitter = require('../utils/EventEmitter');
const Logger = require('../utils/Logger');
const Validator = require('../utils/Validator');

class FeatureFlagManager extends EventEmitter {
  constructor(storage, analytics) {
    super();
    this.storage = storage;
    this.analytics = analytics;
    this.flags = new Map();
    this.logger = new Logger('FeatureFlagManager');
    this.initialized = false;
    
    // Cache para performance
    this.userCache = new Map();
    this.cacheTTL = 30000; // 30 segundos
  }

  async initialize() {
    try {
      await this.loadAllFlags();
      this.startCacheCleanup();
      this.initialized = true;
      this.logger.info('FeatureFlagManager inicializado');
      this.emit('initialized');
    } catch (error) {
      this.logger.error('Falha na inicialização:', error);
      throw error;
    }
  }

  async loadAllFlags() {
    const flags = await this.storage.getAllFlags();
    flags.forEach(flag => {
      this.flags.set(flag.key, this.normalizeFlag(flag));
    });
  }

  normalizeFlag(flag) {
    return {
      key: flag.key,
      name: flag.name,
      description: flag.description,
      enabled: flag.enabled,
      type: flag.type || 'boolean',
      defaultValue: flag.defaultValue || false,
      
      // Rollout config
      rollout: {
        percentage: flag.rollout?.percentage || 0,
        strategy: flag.rollout?.strategy || 'random',
        buckets: flag.rollout?.buckets || 1000,
        seed: flag.rollout?.seed || flag.key
      },
      
      // Segment targeting
      segments: flag.segments || [],
      
      // User targeting
      userTargeting: flag.userTargeting || {
        userIds: [],
        userAttributes: {}
      },
      
      // Schedule
      schedule: flag.schedule || {
        startDate: null,
        endDate: null,
        timezone: 'UTC'
      },
      
      // Variants para flags multivariadas
      variants: flag.variants || [],
      
      // Metadata
      createdAt: flag.createdAt || new Date().toISOString(),
      updatedAt: flag.updatedAt || new Date().toISOString(),
      createdBy: flag.createdBy || 'system',
      tags: flag.tags || []
    };
  }

  async isEnabled(flagKey, context = {}) {
    if (!this.initialized) {
      this.logger.warn('Manager não inicializado, retornando default');
      return this.getDefaultValue(flagKey);
    }

    const flag = this.flags.get(flagKey);
    if (!flag) {
      this.logger.debug(`Flag não encontrada: ${flagKey}`);
      return this.getDefaultValue(flagKey);
    }

    // Verificar schedule
    if (!this.isWithinSchedule(flag)) {
      return flag.defaultValue;
    }

    // Verificar se flag está habilitada
    if (!flag.enabled) {
      return flag.defaultValue;
    }

    // Verificar targeting de usuário específico
    if (this.isUserExplicitlyTargeted(flag, context.userId)) {
      return true;
    }

    // Verificar segmentos
    if (flag.segments.length > 0) {
      const isInSegment = await this.evaluateSegments(flag.segments, context);
      if (!isInSegment) {
        return flag.defaultValue;
      }
    }

    // Aplicar rollout
    const rolloutValue = this.calculateRollout(flag, context);
    
    // Registrar analytics
    this.trackEvaluation(flagKey, context, rolloutValue);
    
    return rolloutValue;
  }

  async getVariant(flagKey, context = {}) {
    const flag = this.flags.get(flagKey);
    if (!flag || flag.type !== 'multivariate') {
      return null;
    }

    if (!await this.isEnabled(flagKey, context)) {
      return flag.defaultValue;
    }

    const rolloutValue = this.calculateRollout(flag, context);
    const variant = this.selectVariant(flag, rolloutValue, context);
    
    this.trackVariant(flagKey, variant, context);
    
    return variant;
  }

  calculateRollout(flag, context) {
    const { strategy, percentage, buckets, seed } = flag.rollout;
    
    switch(strategy) {
      case 'random':
        return this.randomRollout(percentage, context);
      case 'consistent':
        return this.consistentRollout(percentage, context, seed);
      case 'gradual':
        return this.gradualRollout(percentage, context);
      case 'canary':
        return this.canaryRollout(percentage, context);
      default:
        return this.randomRollout(percentage, context);
    }
  }

  randomRollout(percentage, context) {
    return Math.random() * 100 < percentage;
  }

  consistentRollout(percentage, context, seed) {
    // Hash consistente baseado no userId ou sessionId
    const identifier = context.userId || context.sessionId || 'anonymous';
    const hash = this.stringToHash(identifier + seed);
    const bucket = hash % 100;
    
    return bucket < percentage;
  }

  stringToHash(str) {
    let hash = 0;
    for (let i = 0; i < str.length; i++) {
      const char = str.charCodeAt(i);
      hash = ((hash << 5) - hash) + char;
      hash = hash & hash; // Convert to 32bit integer
    }
    return Math.abs(hash);
  }

  async evaluateSegments(segmentRules, context) {
    // Implementação de avaliação de segmentos
    // Suporta: AND, OR, NOT, operadores de comparação
    for (const rule of segmentRules) {
      const result = await this.evaluateRule(rule, context);
      if (!result) return false;
    }
    return true;
  }

  async evaluateRule(rule, context) {
    // Implementação de regras complexas
    switch (rule.operator) {
      case 'equals':
        return context[rule.property] === rule.value;
      case 'contains':
        return context[rule.property]?.includes?.(rule.value);
      case 'greaterThan':
        return context[rule.property] > rule.value;
      case 'lessThan':
        return context[rule.property] < rule.value;
      case 'in':
        return rule.value.includes(context[rule.property]);
      case 'regex':
        return new RegExp(rule.value).test(context[rule.property]);
      default:
        return false;
    }
  }

  trackEvaluation(flagKey, context, result) {
    if (this.analytics) {
      this.analytics.track('feature_flag_evaluated', {
        flagKey,
        userId: context.userId,
        sessionId: context.sessionId,
        result,
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
        context: this.sanitizeContext(context)
      });
    }
  }

  sanitizeContext(context) {
    // Remove dados sensíveis
    const sanitized = { ...context };
    delete sanitized.password;
    delete sanitized.token;
    delete sanitized.creditCard;
    return sanitized;
  }

  startCacheCleanup() {
    setInterval(() => {
      this.userCache.clear();
    }, this.cacheTTL);
  }

  async createFlag(flagData) {
    const validation = Validator.validateFlag(flagData);
    if (!validation.valid) {
      throw new Error(`Flag inválida: ${validation.errors.join(', ')}`);
    }

    const flag = this.normalizeFlag(flagData);
    await this.storage.saveFlag(flag);
    this.flags.set(flag.key, flag);
    
    this.emit('flag_created', flag);
    this.logger.info(`Flag criada: ${flag.key}`);
    
    return flag;
  }

  async updateFlag(flagKey, updates) {
    const flag = this.flags.get(flagKey);
    if (!flag) {
      throw new Error(`Flag não encontrada: ${flagKey}`);
    }

    const updatedFlag = { ...flag, ...updates, updatedAt: new Date().toISOString() };
    await this.storage.updateFlag(flagKey, updatedFlag);
    this.flags.set(flagKey, updatedFlag);
    
    this.emit('flag_updated', updatedFlag);
    this.logger.info(`Flag atualizada: ${flagKey}`);
    
    return updatedFlag;
  }

  async deleteFlag(flagKey) {
    await this.storage.deleteFlag(flagKey);
    this.flags.delete(flagKey);
    
    this.emit('flag_deleted', flagKey);
    this.logger.info(`Flag removida: ${flagKey}`);
  }

  getAllFlags() {
    return Array.from(this.flags.values());
  }

  getFlag(flagKey) {
    return this.flags.get(flagKey);
  }

  getDefaultValue(flagKey) {
    const flag = this.flags.get(flagKey);
    return flag ? flag.defaultValue : false;
  }

  isWithinSchedule(flag) {
    if (!flag.schedule.startDate && !flag.schedule.endDate) {
      return true;
    }

    const now = new Date();
    const start = flag.schedule.startDate ? new Date(flag.schedule.startDate) : null;
    const end = flag.schedule.endDate ? new Date(flag.schedule.endDate) : null;

    if (start && now < start) return false;
    if (end && now > end) return false;
    
    return true;
  }

  isUserExplicitlyTargeted(flag, userId) {
    if (!userId) return false;
    return flag.userTargeting.userIds.includes(userId);
  }

  selectVariant(flag, rolloutValue, context) {
    if (!rolloutValue) return flag.defaultValue;
    
    const identifier = context.userId || context.sessionId || 'anonymous';
    const hash = this.stringToHash(identifier + flag.key);
    const bucket = hash % 100;
    
    let accumulated = 0;
    for (const variant of flag.variants) {
      accumulated += variant.weight;
      if (bucket < accumulated) {
        return variant.value;
      }
    }
    
    return flag.defaultValue;
  }

  trackVariant(flagKey, variant, context) {
    if (this.analytics) {
      this.analytics.track('feature_flag_variant_selected', {
        flagKey,
        variant,
        userId: context.userId,
        sessionId: context.sessionId,
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
      });
    }
  }
}

module.exports = FeatureFlagManager;
```

## 2. Core - RolloutStrategies.js

```javascript
// src/core/RolloutStrategies.js
class RolloutStrategies {
  static strategies = {
    random: {
      name: 'Random',
      description: 'Distribuição aleatória uniforme',
      evaluate: (percentage, context) => Math.random() * 100 < percentage
    },
    
    consistent: {
      name: 'Consistent Hashing',
      description: 'Usuários consistentemente na mesma cohort',
      evaluate: (percentage, context, seed) => {
        const identifier = context.userId || context.sessionId || 'anonymous';
        const hash = RolloutStrategies.hashString(identifier + seed);
        return hash % 100 < percentage;
      }
    },
    
    gradual: {
      name: 'Gradual Rollout',
      description: 'Incrementa gradualmente baseado no tempo',
      evaluate: (percentage, context, seed, flagCreatedAt) => {
        const now = new Date();
        const created = new Date(flagCreatedAt);
        const hoursSinceCreation = (now - created) / (1000 * 60 * 60);
        
        // Aumenta 5% por hora até atingir o percentage target
        const gradualPercentage = Math.min(percentage, hoursSinceCreation * 5);
        return Math.random() * 100 < gradualPercentage;
      }
    },
    
    canary: {
      name: 'Canary Release',
      description: 'Libera para grupos específicos primeiro',
      evaluate: (percentage, context) => {
        // Canary baseado em atributos do usuário
        const userGroup = context.userAttributes?.group || 'default';
        const canaryGroups = ['beta_testers', 'employees', 'vip'];
        
        if (canaryGroups.includes(userGroup)) {
          return true;
        }
        
        return Math.random() * 100 < percentage;
      }
    },
    
    percentageByAttribute: {
      name: 'Percentage by Attribute',
      description: 'Rollout baseado em atributo específico',
      evaluate: (percentage, context, attribute) => {
        const value = context[attribute];
        if (!value) return false;
        
        const hash = RolloutStrategies.hashString(value.toString());
        return hash % 100 < percentage;
      }
    }
  };

  static hashString(str) {
    let hash = 0;
    for (let i = 0; i < str.length; i++) {
      const char = str.charCodeAt(i);
      hash = ((hash << 5) - hash) + char;
      hash = hash & hash;
    }
    return Math.abs(hash);
  }

  static getStrategy(strategyName) {
    return this.strategies[strategyName] || this.strategies.random;
  }

  static getAllStrategies() {
    return Object.entries(this.strategies).map(([key, strategy]) => ({
      id: key,
      ...strategy
    }));
  }

  static validateStrategyConfig(strategyName, config) {
    const strategy = this.strategies[strategyName];
    if (!strategy) {
      return { valid: false, error: `Estratégia desconhecida: ${strategyName}` };
    }

    // Validações específicas por estratégia
    switch(strategyName) {
      case 'consistent':
        if (!config.seed) {
          return { valid: false, error: 'Seed é obrigatória para estratégia consistent' };
        }
        break;
      case 'percentageByAttribute':
        if (!config.attribute) {
          return { valid: false, error: 'Attribute é obrigatório para percentageByAttribute' };
        }
        break;
    }

    return { valid: true };
  }
}

module.exports = RolloutStrategies;
```

## 3. Core - SegmentManager.js

```javascript
// src/core/SegmentManager.js
const Logger = require('../utils/Logger');

class SegmentManager {
  constructor(storage) {
    this.storage = storage;
    this.segments = new Map();
    this.logger = new Logger('SegmentManager');
  }

  async initialize() {
    await this.loadAllSegments();
    this.logger.info('SegmentManager inicializado');
  }

  async loadAllSegments() {
    const segments = await this.storage.getAllSegments();
    segments.forEach(segment => {
      this.segments.set(segment.id, segment);
    });
  }

  async evaluateUserInSegment(segmentId, userContext) {
    const segment = this.segments.get(segmentId);
    if (!segment) {
      this.logger.warn(`Segmento não encontrado: ${segmentId}`);
      return false;
    }

    return this.evaluateRules(segment.rules, userContext);
  }

  async evaluateRules(rules, context) {
    if (!rules || rules.length === 0) {
      return true;
    }

    // Suporta operadores lógicos: AND, OR, NOT
    return this.evaluateLogicalExpression(rules, context);
  }

  evaluateLogicalExpression(expression, context) {
    if (typeof expression === 'object' && expression.operator) {
      switch (expression.operator.toUpperCase()) {
        case 'AND':
          return expression.rules.every(rule => 
            this.evaluateLogicalExpression(rule, context)
          );
        
        case 'OR':
          return expression.rules.some(rule => 
            this.evaluateLogicalExpression(rule, context)
          );
        
        case 'NOT':
          return !this.evaluateLogicalExpression(expression.rule, context);
        
        default:
          return this.evaluateCondition(expression, context);
      }
    }
    
    return this.evaluateCondition(expression, context);
  }

  evaluateCondition(condition, context) {
    const { property, operator, value } = condition;
    const actualValue = this.getNestedProperty(context, property);
    
    switch (operator) {
      case 'equals':
        return actualValue == value;
      
      case 'strictEquals':
        return actualValue === value;
      
      case 'notEquals':
        return actualValue != value;
      
      case 'contains':
        return actualValue?.includes?.(value);
      
      case 'notContains':
        return !actualValue?.includes?.(value);
      
      case 'startsWith':
        return actualValue?.startsWith?.(value);
      
      case 'endsWith':
        return actualValue?.endsWith?.(value);
      
      case 'greaterThan':
        return actualValue > value;
      
      case 'greaterThanOrEquals':
        return actual

### [Sessão Paralela: Compliance]
```javascript
// src/compliance/data-governance.js
/**
 * DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core
 * Framework de Governança de Dados Pessoais
 * Compliance: LGPD, GDPR, SOC2, ISO 27001
 */

const fs = require('fs').promises;
const path = require('path');
const crypto = require('crypto');
const { Database } = require('sqlite3');
const { promisify } = require('util');

class DataGovernanceFramework {
    constructor() {
        this.dataCatalog = new Map();
        this.retentionPolicies = new Map();
        this.auditTrail = [];
        this.init();
    }

    async init() {
        await this.loadDataCatalog();
        await this.loadRetentionPolicies();
        await this.setupAuditLogger();
        console.log('✅ Framework de Governança inicializado');
    }

    // 1. CATALOGO DE DADOS PESSOAIS
    async loadDataCatalog() {
        try {
            const catalogPath = path.join(__dirname, '../data/catalog.json');
            const data = await fs.readFile(catalogPath, 'utf8');
            this.dataCatalog = new Map(Object.entries(JSON.parse(data)));
        } catch (error) {
            // Catálogo padrão se não existir
            this.dataCatalog = new Map([
                ['user_profile', {
                    category: 'Identificação',
                    fields: ['name', 'email', 'cpf', 'phone', 'birth_date'],
                    sensitivity: 'high',
                    purpose: 'Autenticação e personalização',
                    legalBasis: 'contract',
                    retentionDays: 730, // 2 anos
                    processor: 'internal'
                }],
                ['user_activity', {
                    category: 'Comportamento',
                    fields: ['ip_address', 'user_agent', 'actions', 'timestamps'],
                    sensitivity: 'medium',
                    purpose: 'Analytics e segurança',
                    legalBasis: 'legitimate_interest',
                    retentionDays: 180, // 6 meses
                    processor: 'internal'
                }],
                ['payment_info', {
                    category: 'Financeiro',
                    fields: ['card_last4', 'card_brand', 'billing_address'],
                    sensitivity: 'high',
                    purpose: 'Processamento de pagamentos',
                    legalBasis: 'contract',
                    retentionDays: 1095, // 3 anos (fiscal)
                    processor: 'stripe'
                }],
                ['llm_interactions', {
                    category: 'Conteúdo',
                    fields: ['prompt', 'response', 'user_id', 'session_id'],
                    sensitivity: 'medium',
                    purpose: 'Melhoria do serviço de IA',
                    legalBasis: 'consent',
                    retentionDays: 90,
                    processor: 'anthropic',
                    aiActClassification: 'limited_risk'
                }]
            ]);
            await this.saveDataCatalog();
        }
    }

    async saveDataCatalog() {
        const catalogPath = path.join(__dirname, '../data/catalog.json');
        const dir = path.dirname(catalogPath);
        await fs.mkdir(dir, { recursive: true });
        
        const catalogObj = Object.fromEntries(this.dataCatalog);
        await fs.writeFile(catalogPath, JSON.stringify(catalogObj, null, 2));
        
        await this.logAudit('CATALOG_UPDATE', {
            action: 'save_catalog',
            entries: this.dataCatalog.size
        });
    }

    // 2. MAPEAMENTO DE DADOS EM TEMPO REAL
    async mapDataFlow(tableName, operation, data) {
        const flowId = crypto.randomBytes(8).toString('hex');
        const timestamp = new Date().toISOString();
        
        const dataFields = this.extractPersonalDataFields(data);
        const classification = this.classifyDataSensitivity(dataFields);
        
        const flowRecord = {
            flowId,
            timestamp,
            table: tableName,
            operation,
            dataFields,
            classification,
            userId: data.user_id || 'system',
            sessionId: data.session_id || crypto.randomBytes(4).toString('hex')
        };

        // Registro imediato no trail
        await this.logAudit('DATA_FLOW', flowRecord);
        
        // Verificação de compliance
        const complianceCheck = await this.checkCompliance(flowRecord);
        
        if (!complianceCheck.valid) {
            await this.handleComplianceViolation(flowRecord, complianceCheck.issues);
        }

        return {
            flowId,
            compliance: complianceCheck,
            requiresConsent: this.requiresConsent(flowRecord)
        };
    }

    extractPersonalDataFields(data) {
        const fields = [];
        const personalDataPatterns = {
            email: /^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]+$/,
            cpf: /^\d{3}\.\d{3}\.\d{3}-\d{2}$/,
            phone: /^(\+55)?\s?(\(?\d{2}\)?)?\s?\d{4,5}-?\d{4}$/,
            birth_date: /^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$/
        };

        const traverse = (obj, path = '') => {
            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(obj)) {
                const currentPath = path ? `${path}.${key}` : key;
                
                if (value && typeof value === 'object') {
                    traverse(value, currentPath);
                } else if (typeof value === 'string') {
                    // Verifica padrões de dados pessoais
                    for (const [type, pattern] of Object.entries(personalDataPatterns)) {
                        if (pattern.test(value)) {
                            fields.push({
                                path: currentPath,
                                type,
                                value: this.maskSensitiveData(type, value)
                            });
                        }
                    }
                    
                    // Verifica por contexto
                    if (key.toLowerCase().includes('name') && value.length > 2) {
                        fields.push({
                            path: currentPath,
                            type: 'name',
                            value: this.maskSensitiveData('name', value)
                        });
                    }
                }
            }
        };

        traverse(data);
        return fields;
    }

    maskSensitiveData(type, value) {
        switch(type) {
            case 'email':
                const [user, domain] = value.split('@');
                return `${user[0]}***@${domain}`;
            case 'cpf':
                return value.replace(/\d/g, '*').replace(/(\d{3})\.(\d{3})\.(\d{3})-(\d{2})/, '$1.$2.$3-**');
            case 'phone':
                return value.replace(/\d(?=\d{4})/g, '*');
            default:
                return value;
        }
    }

    // 3. POLÍTICAS DE RETENÇÃO E EXCLUSÃO
    async loadRetentionPolicies() {
        this.retentionPolicies = new Map([
            ['user_profile', {
                retentionDays: 730,
                autoDeletion: true,
                legalRequirement: 'Art. 7º LGPD - Execução de contrato',
                deletionMethod: 'anonymization',
                exceptions: ['fiscal_records']
            }],
            ['user_activity', {
                retentionDays: 180,
                autoDeletion: true,
                legalRequirement: 'Legítimo interesse - segurança',
                deletionMethod: 'hard_delete',
                backupRetention: 30
            }],
            ['llm_interactions', {
                retentionDays: 90,
                autoDeletion: true,
                legalRequirement: 'Consentimento específico',
                deletionMethod: 'pseudonymization',
                aiActRequirement: 'Transparência - Art. 52 EU AI Act'
            }],
            ['audit_logs', {
                retentionDays: 365 * 5, // 5 anos
                autoDeletion: false,
                legalRequirement: 'Art. 42 LGPD - Responsabilização',
                deletionMethod: 'archival'
            }]
        ]);
    }

    async applyRetentionPolicy(tableName, recordId) {
        const policy = this.retentionPolicies.get(tableName);
        if (!policy || !policy.autoDeletion) return;

        const recordAge = await this.getRecordAge(tableName, recordId);
        
        if (recordAge > policy.retentionDays) {
            await this.executeDeletion(tableName, recordId, policy.deletionMethod);
            
            await this.logAudit('RETENTION_APPLIED', {
                table: tableName,
                recordId,
                ageDays: recordAge,
                policy: policy.retentionDays,
                method: policy.deletionMethod
            });
        }
    }

    async executeDeletion(tableName, recordId, method) {
        const db = await this.getDatabase();
        
        switch(method) {
            case 'anonymization':
                await db.run(
                    `UPDATE ${tableName} SET 
                     personal_data = NULL,
                     anonymized_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
                     anonymization_method = 'retention_policy'
                     WHERE id = ?`,
                    [recordId]
                );
                break;
                
            case 'pseudonymization':
                const pseudonym = crypto.randomBytes(16).toString('hex');
                await db.run(
                    `UPDATE ${tableName} SET 
                     user_id = ?,
                     pseudonymized_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
                     WHERE id = ?`,
                    [pseudonym, recordId]
                );
                break;
                
            case 'hard_delete':
                await db.run(
                    `DELETE FROM ${tableName} WHERE id = ?`,
                    [recordId]
                );
                break;
        }
    }

    // 4. AUDIT TRAIL COMPLETO
    async setupAuditLogger() {
        const auditDbPath = path.join(__dirname, '../data/audit.db');
        this.auditDb = new Database(auditDbPath);
        
        await promisify(this.auditDb.run.bind(this.auditDb))(`
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS audit_trail (
                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                event_type TEXT NOT NULL,
                event_data JSON NOT NULL,
                timestamp DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
                user_id TEXT,
                session_id TEXT,
                ip_address TEXT,
                user_agent TEXT,
                checksum TEXT
            )
        `);
        
        await promisify(this.auditDb.run.bind(this.auditDb))(`
            CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_audit_timestamp 
            ON audit_trail(timestamp)
        `);
        
        await promisify(this.auditDb.run.bind(this.auditDb))(`
            CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_audit_user 
            ON audit_trail(user_id, timestamp)
        `);
    }

    async logAudit(eventType, eventData) {
        const checksum = crypto
            .createHash('sha256')
            .update(JSON.stringify(eventData) + Date.now())
            .digest('hex');
        
        const auditRecord = {
            event_type: eventType,
            event_data: JSON.stringify(eventData),
            timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
            checksum
        };
        
        await promisify(this.auditDb.run.bind(this.auditDb))(
            `INSERT INTO audit_trail 
             (event_type, event_data, timestamp, checksum)
             VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?)`,
            [auditRecord.event_type, auditRecord.event_data, 
             auditRecord.timestamp, auditRecord.checksum]
        );
        
        this.auditTrail.push(auditRecord);
        
        // Manter apenas últimos 1000 em memória
        if (this.auditTrail.length > 1000) {
            this.auditTrail = this.auditTrail.slice(-1000);
        }
    }

    // 5. VERIFICAÇÕES DE COMPLIANCE
    async checkCompliance(flowRecord) {
        const issues = [];
        
        // Verificação LGPD - Base legal
        if (flowRecord.dataFields.length > 0) {
            const hasLegalBasis = await this.validateLegalBasis(
                flowRecord.table, 
                flowRecord.operation
            );
            if (!hasLegalBasis) {
                issues.push({
                    code: 'LGPD_ART7',
                    severity: 'high',
                    message: 'Operação sem base legal definida'
                });
            }
        }
        
        // Verificação EU AI Act para interações com LLM
        if (flowRecord.table.includes('llm_')) {
            const aiActCompliance = await this.checkAIActCompliance(flowRecord);
            if (!aiActCompliance.valid) {
                issues.push(...aiActCompliance.issues);
            }
        }
        
        // Verificação de minimização de dados
        const minimizationCheck = this.checkDataMinimization(flowRecord);
        if (!minimizationCheck.valid) {
            issues.push(minimizationCheck.issue);
        }
        
        return {
            valid: issues.length === 0,
            issues,
            timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
            flowId: flowRecord.flowId
        };
    }

    async checkAIActCompliance(flowRecord) {
        const issues = [];
        const catalogEntry = this.dataCatalog.get('llm_interactions');
        
        if (catalogEntry.aiActClassification === 'high_risk') {
            // Verificar supervisão humana para alto risco
            const hasHumanOversight = flowRecord.dataFields.some(
                f => f.path.includes('human_review')
            );
            
            if (!hasHumanOversight) {
                issues.push({
                    code: 'EU_AI_ACT_52',
                    severity: 'high',
                    message: 'Sistema de alto risco sem supervisão humana'
                });
            }
        }
        
        // Transparência - usuário deve saber que está interagindo com IA
        if (!flowRecord.dataFields.some(f => f.path.includes('ai_disclosure'))) {
            issues.push({
                code: 'EU_AI_ACT_13',
                severity: 'medium',
                message: 'Falta indicação de interação com IA'
            });
        }
        
        return {
            valid: issues.length === 0,
            issues
        };
    }

    // 6. DASHBOARD DE GOVERNANÇA
    async generateGovernanceReport() {
        const report = {
            generated_at: new Date().toISOString(),
            data_catalog: {
                total_categories: this.dataCatalog.size,
                high_sensitivity: Array.from(this.dataCatalog.values())
                    .filter(d => d.sensitivity === 'high').length,
                medium_sensitivity: Array.from(this.dataCatalog.values())
                    .filter(d => d.sensitivity === 'medium').length
            },
            retention_status: await this.getRetentionStatus(),
            compliance_checks: await this.getComplianceMetrics(),
            pending_deletions: await this.getPendingDeletions(),
            audit_coverage: await this.getAuditCoverage()
        };
        
        return report;
    }

    async getRetentionStatus() {
        const db = await this.getDatabase();
        const status = {};
        
        for (const [table, policy] of this.retentionPolicies) {
            const result = await promisify(db.get.bind(db))(
                `SELECT COUNT(*) as total,
                 SUM(CASE WHEN 
                     julianday('now') - julianday(created_at) > ?
                     THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as overdue
                 FROM ${table}`,
                [policy.retentionDays]
            );
            
            status[table] = {
                total: result.total,
                overdue: result.overdue,
                policy_days: policy.retentionDays,
                compliance: result.overdue === 0 ? 'compliant' : 'non_compliant'
            };
        }
        
        return status;
    }

    // 7. WEBHOOKS PARA SISTEMAS EXTERNOS
    async notifyDPO(event, data) {
        // Integração com sistema do DPO
        const webhookUrl = process.env.DPO_WEBHOOK_URL;
        
        if (webhookUrl) {
            try {
                const response = await fetch(webhookUrl, {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: {
                        'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                        'X-Compliance-Signature': this.generateSignature(data)
                    },
                    body: JSON.stringify({
                        event,
                        data,
                        timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
                        system: 'DIYAPP_V11'
                    })
                });
                
                await this.logAudit('DPO_NOTIFICATION', {
                    event,
                    status: response.status,
                    timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
                });
            } catch (error) {
                console.error('Erro notificação DPO:', error);
                await this.logAudit('DPO_NOTIFICATION_ERROR', {
                    event,
                    error: error.message
                });
            }
        }
    }

    generateSignature(data) {
        const secret = process.env.COMPLIANCE_SECRET;
        return crypto
            .createHmac('sha256', secret)
            .update(JSON.stringify(data))
            .digest('hex');
    }

    // Métodos auxiliares
    async getDatabase() {
        if (!this.mainDb) {
            const dbPath = path.join(__dirname, '../data/main.db');
            this.mainDb = new Database(dbPath);
        }
        return this.mainDb;
    }

    classifyDataSensitivity(fields) {
        const hasHighSensitivity = fields.some(f => 
            ['cpf', 'card_number', 'health_data'].includes(f.type)
        );
        
        const hasMediumSensitivity = fields.some(f =>
            ['email', 'phone', 'address'].includes(f.type)
        );
        
        if (hasHighSensitivity) return 'high';
        if (hasMediumSensitivity) return 'medium';
        return 'low';
    }

    requiresConsent(flowRecord) {
        const catalogEntry = this.dataCatalog.get(flowRecord.table);
        return catalogEntry && catalogEntry.legalBasis === 'consent';
    }

    async validateLegalBasis(tableName, operation) {
        const catalogEntry = this.dataCatalog.get(tableName);
        if (!catalogEntry) return false;
        
        // Verificar se a operação é compatível com a base legal
        const validOperations = {
            'contract': ['CREATE', 'UPDATE', 'READ'],
            'consent': ['CREATE', 'DELETE'],
            'legitimate_interest': ['CREATE', 'READ'],
            'legal_obligation': ['CREATE', 'UPDATE', 'RETAIN']
        };
        
        return validOperations[catalogEntry.legalBasis]?.includes(operation) || false;
    }

    checkDataMinimization

### [Sessão Paralela: Inovação]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Sistema de Feature Flags Avançado

Vou implementar um sistema completo de feature flags com rollout gradual, targeting por segmentos e analytics integrado. O sistema será 100% autônomo e pronto para produção.

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
feature-flags-system/
├── index.html                    # Dashboard principal
├── package.json                  # Dependências
├── .env.example                  # Variáveis de ambiente
├── src/
│   ├── server.js                 # Servidor principal
│   ├── database/
│   │   ├── db.js                 # Configuração do banco
│   │   └── migrations/           # Migrações do banco
│   ├── controllers/
│   │   ├── flagsController.js    # Controller de flags
│   │   └── analyticsController.js # Controller de analytics
│   ├── models/
│   │   ├── FeatureFlag.js        # Modelo de feature flag
│   │   ├── Segment.js            # Modelo de segmentos
│   │   └── Event.js              # Modelo de eventos
│   ├── services/
│   │   ├── flagService.js        # Serviço de flags
│   │   ├── segmentService.js     # Serviço de segmentos

# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Framework de Governança de Dados

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-governance/
├── src/
│   ├── controllers/
│   │   ├── dataGovernanceController.js
│   │   └── auditController.js
│   ├── models/

│   │   ├── AuditTrail.js

│   │   ├── dataMappingService.js
│   │   ├── retentionService.js
│   │   └── complianceService.js

```json
{
  "name": "diyapp-governance",
  "version": "1.0.0",
  "description": "Framework de Governança de Dados - LGPD Compliance",
  "main": "server.js",
  "scripts": {
    "start": "node server.js",
    "dev": "nodemon server.js",
    "migrate": "node database/migrate.js",
    "seed": "node database/seed.js",
    "audit-report": "node scripts/generateAuditReport.js"

    "express": "^4.18.2",

## 2. Configuração de Governança (governanceConfig.js)

```javascript
// src/config/governanceConfig.js
module.exports = {
  // Categorias de dados pessoais conforme LGPD
  DATA_CATEGORIES: {
    IDENTIFICATION: {
      code: 'IDENT',
      description: 'Dados de identificação',
      examples: ['nome', 'CPF', 'RG', 'data_nascimento', 'foto'],
      sensitivity: 'HIGH',
      retentionBase: 'CONTRACT'
    },
    CONTACT: {
      code: 'CONTACT',
      description: 'Dados de contato',
      examples: ['email', 'telefone', 'endereço'],
      sensitivity: 'MEDIUM',
      retentionBase: 'CONTRACT'
    },
    FINANCIAL: {
      code: 'FIN',
      description: 'Dados financeiros',
      examples: ['cartão_credito', 'conta_bancaria', 'transações'],
      sensitivity: 'HIGH',
      retentionBase: 'LEGAL'
    },
    BEHAVIORAL: {
      code: 'BEHAV',
      description: 'Dados comportamentais',
      examples: ['histórico_navegação', 'preferências', 'logs_acesso'],
      sensitivity: 'MEDIUM',
      retentionBase: 'LEGITIMATE_INTEREST'
    },
    SENSITIVE: {
      code: 'SENS',
      description: 'Dados sensíveis (LGPD Art. 5º II)',
      examples: ['origem_racial', 'crença_religiosa', 'saúde', 'vida_sexual'],
      sensitivity: 'CRITICAL',
      retentionBase: 'EXPLICIT_CONSENT'
    },
    ANONYMIZED: {
      code: 'ANON',
      description: 'Dados anonimizados',
      examples: ['hash_usuario', 'dados_agregados'],
      sensitivity: 'LOW',
      retentionBase: 'LEGITIMATE_INTEREST'
    }
  },

  // Bases legais conforme LGPD Art. 7
  LEGAL_BASES: {
    CONSENT: {
      code: 'CONSENT',
      description: 'Consentimento do titular',
      requires: ['record_consent', 'withdrawable', 'granular']
    },
    CONTRACT: {
      code: 'CONTRACT',
      description: 'Execução de contrato',
      requires: ['contract_reference']
    },
    LEGAL: {
      code: 'LEGAL',
      description: 'Obrigação legal',
      requires: ['law_reference']
    },
    LEGITIMATE_INTEREST: {
      code: 'LEGITIMATE',
      description: 'Interesse legítimo',
      requires: ['balancing_test', 'opt_out']
    },
    VITAL: {
      code: 'VITAL',
      description: 'Proteção da vida',
      requires: ['emergency_context']
    }
  },

  // Políticas de retenção padrão
  DEFAULT_RETENTION_POLICIES: {
    IDENT: {
      duration: 730, // 2 anos após término do contrato
      unit: 'DAYS',
      justification: 'Prazo prescricional para ações contratuais',
      autoDelete: true
    },
    CONTACT: {
      duration: 365, // 1 ano após último contato
      unit: 'DAYS',
      justification: 'Manutenção de canal de comunicação',
      autoDelete: true
    },
    FIN: {
      duration: 1825, // 5 anos (obrigação fiscal)
      unit: 'DAYS',
      justification: 'Art. 173 da Lei 6.404/76 e obrigações fiscais',
      autoDelete: false // Requer revisão manual
    },
    BEHAV: {
      duration: 180,
      unit: 'DAYS',
      justification: 'Melhoria de serviços',
      autoDelete: true
    },
    SENS: {
      duration: 90,
      unit: 'DAYS',
      justification: 'Minimização de risco',
      autoDelete: true
    }
  },

  // Configurações de auditoria
  AUDIT_CONFIG: {
    retentionDays: 1825, // 5 anos
    logLevels: ['CREATE', 'READ', 'UPDATE', 'DELETE', 'EXPORT', 'CONSENT_CHANGE'],
    sensitiveOperations: ['DELETE', 'EXPORT', 'CONSENT_CHANGE']
  }
};
```

## 3. Modelo de Inventário de Dados (DataInventory.js)

```javascript
// src/models/DataInventory.js
const { DataTypes } = require('sequelize');
const sequelize = require('../config/database');
const config = require('../config/governanceConfig');

const DataInventory = sequelize.define('DataInventory', {
  id: {
    type: DataTypes.UUID,
    defaultValue: DataTypes.UUIDV4,
    primaryKey: true
  },
  dataField: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING(100),
    allowNull: false,
    unique: true
  },
  description: {
    type: DataTypes.TEXT,
    allowNull: false
  },
  dataCategory: {
    type: DataTypes.ENUM(Object.keys(config.DATA_CATEGORIES)),
    allowNull: false
  },
  sensitivityLevel: {
    type: DataTypes.ENUM(['LOW', 'MEDIUM', 'HIGH', 'CRITICAL']),
    allowNull: false
  },
  legalBasis: {
    type: DataTypes.ENUM(Object.keys(config.LEGAL_BASES)),
    allowNull: false
  },
  collectionPoint: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING(200),
    allowNull: false
  },
  purpose: {
    type: DataTypes.TEXT,
    allowNull: false
  },
  retentionPolicyId: {
    type: DataTypes.UUID,
    references: {
      model: 'RetentionPolicies',
      key: 'id'
    }
  },
  sharedWith: {
    type: DataTypes.JSON,
    defaultValue: []
  },
  dpiRequired: {
    type: DataTypes.BOOLEAN,
    defaultValue: false
  },
  dpiCompleted: {
    type: DataTypes.BOOLEAN,
    defaultValue: false
  },
  lastReviewDate: {
    type: DataTypes.DATE
  },
  nextReviewDate: {
    type: DataTypes.DATE
  },
  status: {
    type: DataTypes.ENUM(['ACTIVE', 'DEPRECATED', 'UNDER_REVIEW']),
    defaultValue: 'ACTIVE'
  }
}, {
  tableName: 'data_inventory',
  timestamps: true,
  indexes: [
    {
      fields: ['dataCategory']
    },
    {
      fields: ['sensitivityLevel']
    },
    {
      fields: ['status']
    }
  ]
});

module.exports = DataInventory;
```

## 4. Modelo de Trilha de Auditoria (AuditTrail.js)

```javascript
// src/models/AuditTrail.js
const { DataTypes } = require('sequelize');
const sequelize = require('../config/database');
const crypto = require('crypto');

const AuditTrail = sequelize.define('AuditTrail', {
  id: {
    type: DataTypes.UUID,
    defaultValue: DataTypes.UUIDV4,
    primaryKey: true
  },
  timestamp: {
    type: DataTypes.DATE,
    defaultValue: DataTypes.NOW,
    allowNull: false
  },
  userId: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING(100),
    allowNull: false
  },
  userRole: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING(50),
    allowNull: false
  },
  action: {
    type: DataTypes.ENUM(['CREATE', 'READ', 'UPDATE', 'DELETE', 'EXPORT', 'CONSENT_CHANGE', 'LOGIN', 'LOGOUT']),
    allowNull: false
  },
  entityType: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING(100),
    allowNull: false
  },
  entityId: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING(100),
    allowNull: false
  },
  dataField: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING(100)
  },
  oldValue: {
    type: DataTypes.TEXT
  },
  newValue: {
    type: DataTypes.TEXT
  },
  ipAddress: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING(45)
  },
  userAgent: {
    type: DataTypes.TEXT
  },
  endpoint: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING(500)
  },
  httpMethod: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING(10)
  },
  statusCode: {
    type: DataTypes.INTEGER
  },
  sessionId: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING(100)
  },
  checksum: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING(64),
    allowNull: false
  }
}, {
  tableName: 'audit_trail',
  timestamps: false,
  hooks: {
    beforeCreate: (auditLog) => {
      // Gerar checksum para integridade dos logs
      const dataToHash = `${auditLog.timestamp}${auditLog.userId}${auditLog.action}${auditLog.entityId}${auditLog.oldValue}${auditLog.newValue}`;
      auditLog.checksum = crypto.createHash('sha256').update(dataToHash).digest('hex');
    }
  },
  indexes: [
    {
      fields: ['timestamp']
    },
    {
      fields: ['userId']
    },
    {
      fields: ['action']
    },
    {
      fields: ['entityType', 'entityId']
    },
    {
      fields: ['checksum']
    }
  ]
});

module.exports = AuditTrail;
```

## 5. Modelo de Políticas de Retenção (RetentionPolicy.js)

```javascript
// src/models/RetentionPolicy.js
const { DataTypes } = require('sequelize');
const sequelize = require('../config/database');

const RetentionPolicy = sequelize.define('RetentionPolicy', {
  id: {
    type: DataTypes.UUID,
    defaultValue: DataTypes.UUIDV4,
    primaryKey: true
  },
  name: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING(100),
    allowNull: false,
    unique: true
  },
  description: {
    type: DataTypes.TEXT,
    allowNull: false
  },
  dataCategory: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING(50),
    allowNull: false
  },
  retentionDuration: {
    type: DataTypes.INTEGER,
    allowNull: false
  },
  retentionUnit: {
    type: DataTypes.ENUM(['DAYS', 'MONTHS', 'YEARS']),
    defaultValue: 'DAYS'
  },
  triggerEvent: {
    type: DataTypes.ENUM(['ACCOUNT_CLOSURE', 'LAST_ACTIVITY', 'CONTRACT_END', 'CONSENT_WITHDRAWAL']),
    allowNull: false
  },
  autoDeletion: {
    type: DataTypes.BOOLEAN,
    defaultValue: true
  },
  anonymizationRequired: {
    type: DataTypes.BOOLEAN,
    defaultValue: false
  },
  legalJustification: {
    type: DataTypes.TEXT,
    allowNull: false
  },
  legalReference: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING(200)
  },
  reviewFrequency: {
    type: DataTypes.INTEGER,
    defaultValue: 365
  },
  lastReviewDate: {
    type: DataTypes.DATE
  },
  nextReviewDate: {
    type: DataTypes.DATE
  },
  isActive: {
    type: DataTypes.BOOLEAN,
    defaultValue: true
  }
}, {
  tableName: 'retention_policies',
  timestamps: true,
  hooks: {
    beforeCreate: (policy) => {
      policy.nextReviewDate = new Date();
      policy.nextReviewDate.setDate(policy.nextReviewDate.getDate() + policy.reviewFrequency);
    }
  }
});

module.exports = RetentionPolicy;
```

## 6. Middleware de Auditoria Automática (auditMiddleware.js)

```javascript
// src/middleware/auditMiddleware.js
const AuditTrail = require('../models/AuditTrail');
const crypto = require('crypto');

const auditMiddleware = (options = {}) => {
  return async (req, res, next) => {
    const startTime = Date.now();
    const originalSend = res.send;
    
    // Capturar resposta
    res.send = function(body) {
      res.send = originalSend;
      res.body = body;
      return res.send(body);
    };

    res.on('finish', async () => {
      try {
        // Determinar ação baseada no método HTTP
        const actionMap = {
          'POST': 'CREATE',
          'GET': 'READ',
          'PUT': 'UPDATE',
          'PATCH': 'UPDATE',
          'DELETE': 'DELETE'
        };

        const action = actionMap[req.method] || 'OTHER';
        
        // Não auditar endpoints públicos ou de saúde
        if (req.path.startsWith('/public') || req.path === '/health') {
          return;
        }

        // Extrair informações do usuário
        const userId = req.user?.id || req.ip || 'system';
        const userRole = req.user?.role || 'anonymous';

        // Extrair entityId da URL ou body
        let entityId = req.params.id;
        if (!entityId && req.body && req.body.id) {
          entityId = req.body.id;
        }

        // Capturar mudanças para operações de UPDATE
        let oldValue = null;
        let newValue = null;
        
        if (action === 'UPDATE' && req.originalData) {
          oldValue = JSON.stringify(req.originalData);
          newValue = JSON.stringify(req.body);
        }

        // Criar registro de auditoria
        await AuditTrail.create({
          timestamp: new Date(),
          userId,
          userRole,
          action,
          entityType: req.baseUrl.replace('/', '') || 'unknown',
          entityId: entityId || 'N/A',
          dataField: options.dataField || null,
          oldValue,
          newValue,
          ipAddress: req.ip,
          userAgent: req.get('User-Agent'),
          endpoint: req.originalUrl,
          httpMethod: req.method,
          statusCode: res.statusCode,
          sessionId: req.sessionID,
          responseTime: Date.now() - startTime
        });

      } catch (error) {
        console.error('Erro ao registrar auditoria:', error);
        // Não falhar a requisição por erro de auditoria
      }
    });

    // Para operações de UPDATE, capturar dados originais
    if (req.method === 'PUT' || req.method === 'PATCH') {
      try {
        // Aqui você implementaria a lógica para buscar dados originais
        // Exemplo: req.originalData = await Model.findById(req.params.id);
      } catch (error) {
        console.error('Erro ao capturar dados originais:', error);
      }
    }

    next();
  };
};

    await AuditTrail.create({
      timestamp: new Date(),
      userId: req.user?.id || 'system',
      userRole: req.user?.role || 'admin',

      entityType:
